[维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告（2022年10月31日）第85期（共 1442人） （六）](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/2022103185-1442_56.html)
------

<div>
<p><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span></span></span></b></p><a name='more'></a><b>续上，第六部分：（<span lang="EN-US">T</span>、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>、<span lang="EN-US">V</span>、<span lang="EN-US">W</span>）</b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b><p></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">T.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">塔多坚参（藏）、塔西甫拉提·特依拜（维）、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谭兵林、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭昌蓉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谭得志</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、谭凤江、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谭海燕、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭秋成、谭顺碧、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">汤艳兰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">唐吉田、唐健群、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐雪英</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、唐英杰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐云淑、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐玉<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">、</span>唐之开、唐竹茵、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐祖群</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陶波、陶玉华、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">滕淑丽</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田宝昌、田碧清、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田世胜、田淑兰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田淑学</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、田晓平、田玉琴、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田云波</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">佟恒飙、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">童雪升</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">图丹（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">图丹•洛桑伦珠（藏）、图丹罗珠（藏）、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">涂爱莲、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庹万学</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">拖合塔尔汗•拖列吾汗（哈萨克族）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">塔多坚参（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲市比如县人，又称塔堆坚参，那曲市比如县仲那寺（或称卓那寺）主任及诵经师，西藏自治区前寺院管理会主任，藏族异见僧人，中国在押良心犯。自幼在西藏自治区拉萨市甘丹寺学习佛法；<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年起，一直在仲那寺出任诵经师，并于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年曾任西藏自治区寺院管理会主任；曾于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年出资建立弘扬藏族宗教与文化的学校，不仅自己为学生授课，还从外地邀请文化教师教学指导，深得僧俗藏人敬重，然而此举及其所付努力却使之成为中共西藏当局严打的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其与仲那寺多人被当地警方抓捕、刑拘，理由是在僧舍里发现存有达赖喇嘛画像及演讲书籍等，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，在被审问、羁押一个月后，即被西藏当局以政治罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，时至今日，其案件所涉实际罪名、开庭受审法院、身体健康状况等概不清晰。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">塔西甫拉提·特依拜（维）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1958</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，维族名<span lang="EN-US">Tashpolat Tiyip</span>，新疆维吾尔自治区伊宁市人，早年曾当过拖拉机手，前中共党员，博士生导师，原自治区有特殊贡献的优秀专家、干旱地区研究专家和享受国务院政府特殊津贴专家，日本立正大学客座教授，学科学术带头人，原新疆大学资源与环境科学学院教师，原新疆大学党委副书记、常委、校长，中国在押政治犯。早年就读于新疆大学地理系，毕业后赴日本东京理科大学攻读硕博连读学位，并于<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年获工学博士学位；<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2010</span>年曾先后任新疆大学地理系主任、新疆大学副校长及新疆大学校长；自<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年至被捕前，曾作为学科带头人负责新疆大学“<span lang="EN-US">211</span>工程”子项目之一“新疆资源环境生态与生物技术”重点学科的<span lang="EN-US">1-3</span>期工程；自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年至被捕前，曾主持研究国家级重点项目<span lang="EN-US">19</span>项，并曾在<span lang="EN-US">PE &amp; RS</span>、地理学报、日本地理研究等国内外学术刊物发表过<span lang="EN-US">200</span>余篇学术论文，出版著作<span lang="EN-US">4</span>部，荣获多项省部级奖；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被不明理由免去新疆大学党委副书记、常委、委员及校长职务；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其在与一群学生前往德国参加会议之时，在北京机场被警方强行带走，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，有人看见其身影出现在新疆当局的一部警方教育片中，后得知被新疆中共当局指控为“两面人”（即中共认为对其政党不忠诚不老实，表里不一，阳奉阴违，欺上瞒下），视为违法；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，被新疆伊宁市法院以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处死刑缓期执行；后因其在狱中表现良好，曾将被减为无期徒刑，但<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月突然又面临立即被处决命运。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谭兵林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省衡阳市祁东县人，教育平权推动者，免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老（俗称“三免”）倡导者之一，维权公民，中国在押政治犯。近年来，曾因长期参与推动教育平权运动，倡导俗称“三免”的免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老的民生要求，以及以义工身份积极参与为良心犯送饭的公益活动等，而被社会正义人士和深受关怀帮助的弱势群体广为认可和赞许；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因在老家湖南省祁东县步云桥镇几处重要地段（含市集中心地段、祁东县政府门口、县人大常委会门口等地）举牌要求民生“三免”，即免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老以及其它要求，遂被当地维稳办人员诱骗至镇政府扣押，后被祁东县警方带走调查；期间，尽管刚开始时被很快就被释放，但同天下午又被祁东县警方带走并恶意扣留<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天，要求其写保证书，保证以后不上街举牌，但被其拒绝；后祁东县教育局正副局长前来与其见面，就其举牌内容中提及的教育问题与其谈判；因其坚持向教育局长当面提出<span lang="EN-US">225 </span>个教育问题，终使对方被迫承诺回去后将就其中的<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个问题进行研讨更新，届时必向其作答；然而时至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其因一直未见教育局副局长所称的“不在学校吃饭的学生可以退伙食费”之公示，遂其前往步云桥<span lang="EN-US">3</span>所学校进行调查取证，结果不仅均未看到退款公示，反而遭到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>所校方人员的驱逐和拒绝；而与此同时，却有学生家长听闻其做实地调查，就向其反映说，学校里每天都卖垃圾食品，严重影响了孩子的身体健康，但校方却为自身利益而任由其发展；鉴此，其立即特发声明，呼吁和要求教育局务必让各学校在校门之外张贴退伙食费公示，否则其将于次日恢复上街举牌；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，因其获悉在押政治犯张展在狱中因绝食抗争而致生命垂危，故而毅然在步云桥镇街头再次勇敢举牌声援，以期能引起中共当局的重视，让病重中的张展获准保外就医；正是基于以上言行，其即引起湖南省衡阳市当局极度不满，并成为需要尽快维稳打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其因故前往海南省海口市，但在海口市火车站出站时却遭到防疫人员的拦截和要求强制做核酸检测；被其拒绝后，其身份证被扣，其本人被长时间限制在火车站不准出站；后经海南公民蓝采儿等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人到火车站为其声援，才终与海口火车站方达成协议，对方不再强制其做核酸检测，但必须被警方遣送回原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因其父母被强行接种新冠疫苗，其到村委会举牌抗议，遂立遭衡阳市祁东县警方抓捕，自此失联；同天其家被查抄，其个人手机和笔记本计算机等被一并抄走；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其父获悉，其已于被抓当天被祁东县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；友人疑指，本次其被抓，凶多吉少，很可能会被起诉和判刑。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谭兵林于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被祁东县检察院批准逮捕。目前羁押在湖南省衡阳市衡东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/2022824.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/2022824.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭昌蓉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，谭昌蓉曾被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，在重庆女子监狱，因一直坚持不“转化”，遭受多种折磨，在四监区（重刑监区，多为死缓和无期徒刑），被强迫做奴工，每天做劳役十几个小时。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日中午，在谭昌蓉家门前站着一个男子，男子说是等人，谭昌蓉搬来凳子叫这男子坐下，随后给这男子讲大法真相、给他真相资料看，那男子马上用手机给太安镇派出所打电话，后来谭昌蓉被非法关押到县拘留所，后被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。后关进庆女子监狱。女子监狱狱警唐安智除指使、纵容刑事犯罪服刑人员对法轮功学员进行刑讯逼供体罚、虐待外，还亲自动手打骂谭昌蓉，长时间用电棍电击她，逼她转化写“五书”。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日谭昌蓉女士结束了三年刑期，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，向重庆市司法局和监狱局实名举报自己在重庆女子监狱受到的迫害，以及女子监狱违犯监狱法的事实。谭昌蓉<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日却再次被绑架，现非法关押在合川看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谭得志：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，英文名：<span lang="EN-US">Tam Tak-chi</span>，绰号“快必”，祖籍广东省广州市白云区，原英属香港籍、现中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，香港新界大埔汀角公民，基督徒，前香港电台节目主持，前香港“选民力量”（政党）成员，原香港“人民力量” （政党）副主席，社会活动家，香港首宗“发表煽动文字”定案当事人，泛民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于香港大学中文系，后又在香港中文大学崇基学院修读神学；毕业后，曾在香港电台担任节目主持，后投身于社会运动，并曾于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年加入香港“选民力量”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年起，开始加入香港“人民力量”，并于次年参与香港占领运动（又称“雨伞运动”）；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾积极参选香港区议会选举，并自此担任“人民力量”副主席；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-7</span>月，因其在出席或主持多个公众集会，以及<span lang="EN-US">29</span>次摆街站宣传和参与立法会选举游行抗议期间，发表了抨击港版国安法和香港社会时弊等言论，并多次高呼“光复香港，时代革命”、“解散警队，刻不容缓”、“五大要求，缺一不可”等口号，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，随被香港国安处警方以涉嫌“发表煽动文字罪”拘捕，指控其“言论不止于合法批评，而是煽动他人不理会国安法、挑战警方的公权力，意图激起对抗情绪，从而获得选票进入立法会”；后其曾申请保释被拒，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，二次申请保释又被拒；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其案在香港粉岭裁判法院被庭审，因其又被指控高喊“光时口号”有港独意味，故而被裁定有<span lang="EN-US">14</span>项罪名成立；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，又被粉岭裁判法院在免除<span lang="EN-US">3</span>罪之后，以“发表煽动文字”、“煽惑他人参与未经批准集结”、“未经批准公众游行”、“拒绝遵从或故意忽略遵从获授权人员作出的命令”等<span lang="EN-US">11</span>项罪名等待宣判；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，终被香港特别行政区区域法院（又称湾仔法院）判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">40</span>个月），并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>港币。目前被羁押于香港荔枝角收押所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_6.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_6.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">谭凤江</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，黑龙江省伊春市人，伊春市五营区五星石矿木制品职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。多年来因信法轮功而惨遭当局逼迫打压。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日曾因到北京参加和平请愿活动，为中共镇压法轮功鸣不平，被伊春市当局处以劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日曾因坚持信仰、宣传法轮功，而被伊春市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并在佳木斯莲江口监狱服刑。期间，曾惨遭狱警和犯人合伙毒打、电击、野蛮灌食等非人折磨，致其左耳被打伤。刑满出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因替其他被抓法轮功信仰者聘请辩护律师，惹怒当地公检法部门，被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日其在哈尔滨市打工期间，被哈尔滨市香坊区安埠街警方突然抓走，次日交由伊春市五营区警方刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被转正式逮捕，关押于伊春市友好区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底，被伊春市五营区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；其不服上诉，后经黑龙江省伊春市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判。目前在哈尔滨市呼兰监狱服刑，据悉其被送进监狱至今，家人未收到任何通知。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谭海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，四川省攀枝花市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，原是攀钢朱矿化验室的化验员。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，谭海燕被中共关押在看守所、劳教所、监狱迫害，累计坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被攀枝花市公安局东区公安分局国保和炳草岗派出所抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被攀枝花市东区法院庭审，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭秋成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，吉林省长春市榆树市人，又名谭秋诚，榆树市秀水乡公民，职业不详，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，维权受害者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月始，因锻炼和信仰法轮功，其个性及价值观大改，尤其是使其从一个自私自利的人变成一个常为他人着想的好人，且改掉了抽烟<span lang="EN-US">/</span>酗酒<span lang="EN-US">/</span>赌博等恶习，故而深受亲朋好友的普遍好评；但自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月起，因法轮功遭到中共政府的残酷迫害，进而破坏了其正常合法的锻炼环境，故其曾多次进京上访，为法轮功讨公道、讨说法；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因在京上访时遭截访，随被长春市驻京办人员遣回原籍，并被送榆树市看守所关押；之后很快被地方当局处以劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，并被关押在九台饮马河劳教所；获释后，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，曾因维护宪法赋予人民的追求信仰自由的权利，以及让更多的世人明白法轮功遭受中共迫害的真相，其曾努力以印刷真相传单和制作小喇叭等方式进行宣传，故而又被长春市公安局政保科警方抓捕，并被以涉邪教罪刑拘于铁北看守所；被押期间，曾惨遭毒打、刑讯逼供和被强迫灌食，最终致其身体严重受损；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其案被长春市榆树市法院庭审，终被以“邪教罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，后在吉林省第二监狱服刑，狱中曾惨遭酷刑折磨和非人道虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，终获刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，又因信仰事宜在长春市被四平市、梨树县和长春市等警方在统一的大抓捕行动中抓走，后与十数人悉数被以涉嫌邪教罪拘捕，但因证据不足，其等案综曾被梨树县检察院数次退回，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名法轮功信仰者案（原有<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人，后有<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被取保，故至此共有<span lang="EN-US">14</span>人）被四平市梨树县法院开庭审理，后被一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪” 统一宣判，其中，其被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元，其余人等亦分获<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月不等刑期；其等多人不服判决，均提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，经吉林省四平市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；其刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。目前在吉林省第二监狱（又称吉林监狱、冯家屯监狱，吉林省吉林市船营区军民路<span lang="EN-US">100</span>号<span lang="EN-US">/</span>吉林省吉林市<span lang="EN-US">315</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">132012</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/7.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭顺碧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">成都市青羊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，谭顺碧在成都市人民公园内给一名保洁工讲法轮功被迫害的真相，送了一本小册子，被构陷，遭到四川省成都市青羊区汪家拐派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，成都市青羊区法院判谭顺碧<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">汤艳兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东江门市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年出生，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午两点多，江门市蓬江区公安局、提东派出所十多个警察抓捕汤艳兰，说是因怀疑她网购的纸张与法轮功有关，并搜查她的住宅和车房。汤艳兰被关押在江门市看守所，家中<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个小孩上学无人接送，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日<span lang="EN-US">3</span>餐都成困难。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被蓬江区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐吉田</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，吉林省延边朝鲜族自治州（以下简称“延边州”）敦化市人，北京市常住居民，前延边第二师范学校（后改制为延边第三中学校）教师，原执业律师，人权律师，《零八宪章》签署者，社会活动家，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾就读于东北师范大学政治系；<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年毕业后，曾在吉林省延边州第二师范学校（<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年始被政府改制为延边第三中学校）从事教师工作<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；自<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年起，调入延边州检察院从事刑事公诉工作，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年间代理了上百起重大公诉案件；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，通过律师资格考试，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，毅然辞去公职，先后在上海、深圳、北京、安徽省等地从事执业律师工作，曾为土地被非法征用受害者、强制拆迁受害者、上访者、三聚氰胺污染受害者等进行法律维权；曾接受过多起法轮功案件的代理辩护（含河北省石家庄市法轮功信仰者黄伟案、郝秋艳夫妇被非法拘禁案、辽宁省沈阳市吴业凤被控告“利用邪教破坏法律实施”案等）；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因推动北京市律师协会直选工作，而被律协宣布为非法，并将其作为主要发起人要求其离开所在律所；同年，曾签署了《零八宪章》；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底，六四前夕，曾因要纪念六四而被北京市警方秘密绑架，先关押在海淀区的体育中心<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天，后又转移到朝阳区某宾馆继续关押到<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，才被释放；正因其频繁为被非法征用土地受害者、艾滋病受害者、法轮功信仰者、人权捍卫者以及其他弱势群体提供法律援助和帮助维权，随受到当局鲜明的打击和政治迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其律师营业执照被北京市司法局以“扰乱庭审纪律”为由吊销，但其仍不惧风险，继续活跃在维权领域，从事社会公共活动及多个相关维权案例（如广西北海白虎头村土地维权系列案、天津王宇律师被迫害案、重庆打黑硏讨会、反酷刑北海硏讨会、对高智晟和范亚峰等人遭酷刑问题进行联署等）的推动与策划；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因当局打击中国茉莉花活动，而被北京市警方二度秘密绑架，并被辗转拘押在北京郊区数个地方，遭长时间剥夺睡眠、饥饿、体罚、殴打等酷刑虐待和审讯，导致其患上肺结核，至今仍需治疗中；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因与多位人权律师前往黑龙江省鸡西市帮助被非法拘禁在“学习班”的法轮功信徒，而被鸡西市警方非法扣押，并处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天，期间，惨遭<span lang="EN-US">10</span>根肋骨被打骨折，牙齿被打断；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，再遭离奇车祸，身体多处被骨折，但当其报案时警方却不予立案，交警也拒不调查，谎称监控器已坏；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，曾因身体疾患欲往香港求医，而被深圳罗湖海关的边检部门以“可能危害国家安全”为由拒绝出境；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因其女儿在日本留学期间患肺结核病重，生命垂危，其遂急欲飞往日本探望和给予照顾，但却在福州机场出关时被边检部门拦截，并在北京市公安局指令下以“恐有危害国家安全”禁止出境；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，又因其预备出席次日的欧盟驻北京代表团举办的国际人权日活动，遂被北京市警方以涉嫌“危害国家安全罪”秘押，自此失联；据悉，其之前被押期间，其曾遭受酷刑，其家人亦遭胁迫而不能发声；迄今，其生命垂危的女儿仍然躺在重症监护室<span lang="EN-US">(ICU)</span>里，期盼、苦等其父能来日本与其见上一面。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐吉田终于和友人通话，他说，他一直在吉林延吉某宾馆，隔壁有专人对其“陪护”，春节都没能回去看父母。对他陪护负责的是吉林省延吉市公安局政治保卫部门。他住的房间没有窗户，通风效果差。长期居住于此，整天昏昏沉沉。他曾要求换一个有窗户、能晒到阳光的房间一直没人解决；胸部结核也早到了应该复查的日期，也没有能去复查。饮食还凑合，在有人陪护的情况下也可以到户外走走，活动一下。据老唐说，他眼前的居住环境和看病这样的问题都没有人理睬，也无法出去向有关部门信访反映解决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/202112.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/202112.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">唐健群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华、唐健群等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员唐健群<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，经广东省揭阳市中级法院二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判。目前在广东省女子监狱（广东省广州市白云区广从四路<span lang="EN-US">52</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510545</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/8.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐雪英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，湖南省郴州市柿竹园法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，郴州柿竹园法轮功学员朱志雄、唐雪英夫妇被警察抓捕到下湄桥洗脑班。朱志雄、唐雪英夫妇被强制坐戴锁铁椅，腰部、双脚全锁住，不能动弹，被锁了<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个多小时。之后，朱志雄被放回家。唐雪英被劫持到郴州市梯子岭看守所，<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，唐雪英被构陷到检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月唐雪英遭郴州市苏仙区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/5/442112.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/5/442112.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <span class="MsoHyperlink"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">唐英杰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1996</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，英文名：<span lang="EN-US">Leon</span>，香港籍人，绰号“重甲”，餐厅侍应生（即服务生），“自由香港”追求者，港版《国安法》下首例获罪被告者，中国在押政治犯。自幼生长在香港；少小时因父母离异，随在就读香港中五（相当于中国内地的高二）毕业后，即在一家餐厅做侍应生（即服务人员）；然而，自其工作以来，适逢港府已越来越呈现出中共大陆化管理，尤其是《国安法》在香港的正式实施，使得香港的民主派政治人士及大批青年学生和爱港普通市民等，纷纷遭到前所未有的严苛打压，并对持续多年的维园六四纪念等集会活动予以警戒与封杀，遂“光复香港，时代革命”口号在民主抗议活动中被频繁高呼、张贴于网上，潦草图写在墙上及印制在从小册子、书籍、贴纸、<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤到咖啡杯等各类物品之上；其因亲眼目睹、参与并深刻体会到在香港民主自由的弥足珍贵和香港社会正在被中共迅速大陆化管理的整体性倒退，遂勇敢地发出呼吁，誓用实际行动践行对原香港已有的民主法制机制及自由民主理念的捍卫；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因其驾驶一辆插有“光复香港，时代革命”旗帜的摩托车冲越警方防线，造成<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名警员受伤，随被港警当场拘捕，后被指控因其车上的旗子口号有“港独”及分裂中国的意味，故被以“分裂国家罪”和“恐怖主义罪”继续羁押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其案在香港高等法院奉香港律政司命令不设陪审团的前提下开庭受审，期间，不仅认定其插旗口号“自然而然的结果”就是构成煽动他人分裂中国，而且认为其将摩托车撞向警员是“故意挑战香港法治的象征”，造成严重社会危害；随后拉锯庭审<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，终被以“煽动他人分裂国家罪”和“恐怖活动罪”合判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，停牌（指禁止驾车）<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年；后其曾对定罪与量刑提起上诉，但<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，知其上诉已撤回；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。目前服刑监狱不详。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/9.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/9.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐云淑：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆维权人士。唐云淑家因房屋被基建毁损及拆迁安置补偿发生纠纷，奶奶曾投河、母亲上吊死亡、丈夫莫名死在重庆长江段朝阳河中，公公也因涉嫌医疗事故死亡，丈夫和公公的尸体都还在殡仪馆不能入土为安。自己只是经常为这些事情信访上访维权。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月唐云淑欲前往公安局信访，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被重庆市丰都县公安局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被丰都县人民检察院以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪批捕，目前羁押在重庆市丰都县看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐云淑寻衅滋事案<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午十点开庭前会议，开完庭前会议接着正式开庭。但会否受疫情影响，还不敢最后确定，开庭前还要落实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/12022825.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/12022825.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://msguancha.com/a/lanmu4/2021/1025/21387.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://msguancha.com/a/lanmu4/2021/1025/21387.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南昆明市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住昆明市西山区西华路<span lang="EN-US">49</span>号，昆明市西华公园负责绿化工作。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。自从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年“<span lang="EN-US">720</span>”中共邪党江泽民集团迫害法轮功学员后，唐玉曾遭到抓捕、判刑、抓捕，多次被毒打等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被抓捕、枉判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被抓捕抄家，在派出所遭到毒打，后“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，唐玉再次遭抓捕，被直接送到昆明市中级法院秘密开庭，以<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年前“取保候审”为所谓案由，及<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月的起诉，判她<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时，唐玉、李海艳两女士在昆明市西山区卢家新村路边向路人散发法轮功宣传品，后被抓捕。当局指控两位善良女士犯了所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被昆明市西山区法院视频开庭，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下达判决书（<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>）云<span lang="EN-US">0112</span>刑初<span lang="EN-US">758</span>号，唐玉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月、罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；李海艳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元。唐玉刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/25/446758.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/25/446758.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐之开：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> 1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，四川省达州市大竹县人，重庆市常住居民，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。因笃信法轮功而屡遭中共四川省及重庆市两地当局长期逼迫与监控打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，因<span lang="EN-US">25</span>名法轮功信仰者同聚四川省达州市大竹县竹阳镇一居民家里阅读法轮功书籍，被人跟踪汇报，随四川省当局立即出动达州市各级警力（含达州市、大竹县、大竹县竹阳西区派出所和北区派出所警方）及“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”办公室成员等多人，以敲门换锁等野蛮非法方式将其悉数抓捕，其亦被视为同案嫌疑人于同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被户籍地四川省大竹县的警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”拘捕；同天，其租住处被查抄，当场搜走其个人现金和打印机、播放器等物品多件，后又将其另两处房产也一并非法查抄；之后，虽有其中<span lang="EN-US">20</span>人先后被警方取保释放，但其及<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功信仰者尚仍被达州市大竹县警方刑拘不放；后其等均被达州市大竹县检察院以涉嫌邪教罪予以批捕，且羁关押于达州市大竹县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人涉邪教案被达州市大竹县法院以远程视频方式统一开庭审理；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人终被该法院一审以“组织和利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”共同宣判，其中，其被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人亦被分别枉法判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月—<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月不等刑期。目前疑似在四川省成都龙泉驿监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/5.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐竹茵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：唐竹茵被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐祖群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日早上，四川泸州市法轮功学员敖启珍、唐祖群、彭昭群、章兴连四人从各自家中被抓捕，随后被抄家，关押看守所，被江阳区法院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，泸州市江阳区法院以惯用的诬陷罪名对四人判刑：唐祖群、敖启珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元；彭昭群、章兴连被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金八千元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，泸州市中级法院对唐祖群、敖启珍、章兴连、彭昭群四名法轮功学员，下达维持泸州市江阳区法院一审原判的裁定。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-13"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-13</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陶波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陶波是南通市一名多年的江海志愿者，经常做好事帮助困难群体，他只不过是受了街道的欺骗，导致巨额投资的经济损失，才去打行政官司，却屡屡遭到枉法裁判，现在固定了法院司法黑幕的证据，反过来就要被坐冤狱。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，陶波收到由南通市开发区法院审理的陶波诉南通市崇川区市场监督管理局不履行法定职责一案的行政裁定书。陶波根据中国庭审直播网及裁定书记载的制作时间发现，该案的两位人民陪审员存在未参加合议庭合议，及发表意见与表决的情形，也就是该案的审判长管丽君已经涉嫌私自制作诉讼文书的违法犯罪行为。南通市公安局开发区公安分局是<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日接受陶波报警的机关，在对人民陪审员李辉和陶波做询问笔录时，并没有认为陶波的行为违法。到同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日接受开发区法院报案，却对陶波以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，陶波的家属收到南通市开发区公安分局的逮捕通知书，称经南通市开发区检察院批准，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">19</span>点对“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”的陶波执行逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陶玉华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。陶玉华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">滕淑丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>出生。黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员。鸡西市法轮功学员周克铭在发放法轮功资料时，被人诬告。鸡西市公安局鸡冠区公安分局国保、永昌派出所、铁西派出所采取跟踪、监控手段，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日抓捕了包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被非法关押在鸡西市看守所<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。包万明、周克铭、滕淑丽，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭鸡东法院以视频的方式开庭，近日得知，包万明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、罚金十万元；滕淑丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元；周克铭被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。滕淑丽刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田宝昌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省沈阳市法轮功学员，家住沈阳市大东区，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚上八点半左右，警察闯入田宝昌的家中，将他铐上手铐，抓捕走。田宝昌家中大量物品被警察抄走。田宝昌被非法关押到和平区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，沈阳市和平区法院对田宝昌非法开庭。田宝昌当场辞退了律师，他为自己做了无罪辩护。后遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。田宝昌现被关押在锦州监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田碧清<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，深圳市福田区七旬法轮功学员。一九五一年出生，大学本科毕业，原深圳某大型国企审计师。田碧清一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。田碧清<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日给户口所在地的福田区园岭街道园东小区工作人员赠送劝善的资料时，遭恶意举报，被警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被深圳市南山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52297216"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田世胜：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52297216;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐山市开平区越河乡西塔村法轮功学员田世胜、田淑兰夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日早晨被警察闯入家中抓捕，两人被秘密开庭，田世胜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、田淑兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。田世胜于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被关押到河北省监狱管理局冀东分局第四监狱。田淑兰于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被绑架至河北省女子监狱。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田世胜刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田淑兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐山市开平区越河乡西塔村法轮功学员田世胜、田淑兰夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日早晨被警察闯入家中抓捕，两人被秘密开庭，田世胜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、田淑兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<a name="_Hlk52322917">田世胜于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被关押到河北省监狱管理局冀东分局第四监狱。</a>田淑兰于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被绑架至河北省女子监狱。田淑兰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">田淑学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1938</span>年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日田淑学被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">田晓平：女，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨双城市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，田晓平等四十余位法轮功学员在双城市城建局一栋家属楼里听被迫害致死的法轮功学员秦月明的妻女讲述法律申诉的艰难经历。遭百名特警催泪瓦斯袭击后抓捕。在哈尔滨市第二看守所特审室，田晓平遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，田晓平被哈尔滨双城法院以破坏法律实施罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。田晓平被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，田晓平的家属探视时，发现她已无法独立行走，不能连续说话，身体不停哆嗦，气若游丝。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">田玉琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">田云波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">51</span>岁，昆明市官渡区双桥村人。曾因修炼法轮功被劳教两年，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，还遭关洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，法轮功学员张晓华到官渡区子君路星云园小区朋友家串门，被警方抓捕，随后张晓华家被搜查。同时被抓捕的还有田云波、李萍等人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日张晓华、李萍、田云波被五华区法院视频庭审，后被判刑：张晓华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，李萍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，田云波<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。田云波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a minor-fareast;">大庆市法轮功学员。佟恒飙<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，准备乘火车去北京女儿家过年，在大庆火车东站遭警察抓捕。关在大庆市看守所，经两次「网络视频开庭」，佟恒飙被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已入狱，遭重刑犯暴打，身体受伤。家人、律师至今一直不得见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">童雪升：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年生，福建省三明市清流县人。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，十三岁的童雪升在集美轻工业学校读书时开始修炼法轮功。二十多年来，童雪升因坚持修炼法轮功，屡遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，十六岁的童雪升被迫从天津轻工学院退学，并被拘留四十天。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，十七岁的童雪升在儒江劳教所被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，二十一岁时，童雪升被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在闽西监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，童雪升被广州市天河区公安分局和棠下派出所警察抓捕，关押到广州市天河看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被广州市海珠区法院判刑，童雪升获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/21/450994.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/21/450994.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">图丹（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县僧人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因手持达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，并呼喊着口号独自游街示威，遂立即被警察拘捕。下落不明。现音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">图丹·洛桑伦珠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海藏人作家，笔名“迪拉丹”<span lang="EN-US">(Dhi Lhaden)</span>。迪拉丹是居住于果洛州的藏人知识分子，作家，曾出版《消极抵抗的艺术》一书。迪拉丹<span lang="EN-US">11</span>岁起游历于藏区各地，在藏区各地的寺院学习过，并且在喇荣五明佛学院学过经。迪拉丹于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被当局拘捕，在<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年后遭到判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日图丹·洛桑伦珠<span lang="EN-US">(</span>音<span lang="EN-US">)</span>，被指控“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”，近日被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">图丹罗珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">藏族，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州（简称甘孜州）石渠县蒙宜乡蒙宜村人，原石渠县一中学教师，藏语言及文化倡导者，知名藏人学者和异见作家，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于中国一所大学，毕业后返回老家石渠县，并在当地的一所中学任教多年；曾因多次针对东西方文学、西藏文学和经济等领域发表藏文及汉文文章，深受读者好评，遂逐渐成为一名受境内学术界认可的藏人作家；然而因其发表反对（或不赞同）中共政府对藏人的同化政策文章，尽管其内容并未违宪，但却触碰到中共当局的敏感神经，以致于甘孜州当局指派石渠县警方多次对其进行警告，并肆意搜查其个人计算机等物品；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其被甘孜州石渠县警方莫名强行带走，自此杳无音讯；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其亲人才被当局告知，其已于同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被四川省甘孜藏族自治州石渠县法院以“分裂国家罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前疑似被羁押于甘孜藏族自治州石渠县看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/46.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/46.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">涂爱莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府法轮功学员。涂爱莲是孝南区新铺镇远大小学退休教师，退休才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，在家帮忙带孙女。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。涂爱莲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 159.5pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庹万学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省广安市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住四川省广安市广安区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日庹万学被抓捕关押。此前，庹万学曾被判重刑，在德阳监狱遭酷刑迫害。后得知，庹万学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，已被关押到乐山嘉州监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">拖合塔尔汗•拖列吾汗（哈萨克族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆 建设兵团底<span lang="EN-US">6</span>师<span lang="EN-US">110</span>团<span lang="EN-US">2</span>连（民族连）职工，因集资兴建了一座清真寺，遂被新疆地方当局拘留，先是被送到当地的“去极端化教育中心”关押和洗脑教育，后又此处直接被拘捕抓走，至今毫无因信。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">U.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">V</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">W.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宛芳、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万红霞、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万筱萍、万正平</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times
