宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乌木别提•卡斯木（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邬成均、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">伍健伟</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宛芳</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年出生，哈尔滨市香坊区税务局办税大厅优秀工作人员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，宛芳被哈尔滨铁路公安局国保处警察入室抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日哈尔滨铁路运输法院以视频的形式，开庭，家属聘请的律师为宛芳做了有理有据的无罪辩护。后得知宛芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">万红霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教一家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，随遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被闯入教学点的芜湖市戈江区警方将包括其在内的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名老师莫名抓走，同时，教学点遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人被视为同案嫌疑人统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被准予取保候审外，万红霞及王明海等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被芜湖市戈江区检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转正式批捕；据悉，其案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万筱萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南昌市西湖区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，万筱萍、杨金凤在永正外街，陈丽萍在站前西路锦峰大酒店门口被东湖公安分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，南昌市西湖区法院送达了对陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤及万金莲的刑事判决书，陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，万金莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。因<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均办理了「取保候审」，刑期均从判决执行之日起算。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万正平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省开江县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">，退休工人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，达州市开江县法轮功学员万正平被当地警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，以取保候审方式放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，万正平被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，开江县国保大队副大队长李翔将万正平抓捕到达州市看守所关押。后获悉其被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被转入四川省成都女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/9/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E7%9C%81%E5%BC%80%E6%B1%9F%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%87%E6%AD%A3%E5%B9%B3%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-434551.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/9/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E7%9C%81%E5%BC%80%E6%B1%9F%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%87%E6%AD%A3%E5%B9%B3%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-434551.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王爱弟</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河北唐山法轮功学员。家住唐山市丰润区白官屯镇田富庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，王爱弟被唐山市丰润区白官屯镇派出所人员抓捕、抄家，被抄走大量私人物品。时隔一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，王爱弟被遵化法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金三千元。现今王爱弟被关押在何处，家属无法知晓。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王爱忠：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，祖籍中国浙江省金华市，现居住在广州，广东著名民主人士，南方街头运动倡导者之一。王爱忠因长期致力于推动南方街头运动，受到广东警方高度关注。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，六四<span lang="EN-US">25</span>周年前夕，王爱忠被广州警方于家中采取强制措施，随后以「涉嫌寻衅滋事罪」刑事拘留，关押在广州天河看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日取保候审释放。王爱忠是近年来一直坚持发声的民主人士，其在<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>上的言论一直被中共当局密切监控。此次被抓捕，很可能是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日中午有人打电话给王爱忠，称其车被刮，诱其下楼，将人带走。随后，九名警察到王爱忠家搜查，向王妻出示了搜查证，搜走<span lang="EN-US">29</span>本书，两台电脑，一部手机。随后，还将王妻传唤到派出所，询问王爱忠的交往及言论情况，并警告勿发声。王爱忠随后遭刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，关押在广州天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉王爱忠案已经移送法院，等待开庭。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王爱忠案原定<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州不公开审理被取消 法院无任何理由和解释。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/2022412_8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/2022412_8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王宝山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">河北唐山法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午，唐山市公安和国保伙同丰润区国保大队长蔺文军，还有丰润区永济街派出所人员到王宝山工作单位，直接把大法弟子王宝山绑架，抢走家门和汽车门钥匙，在王宝山家没人的情况下，直接非法抄走家中的电脑和七、八台打印机，还有准备给儿子买房子的钱，中午其没修炼的妻子回家，也被绑架到市公安局，下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点多，才放其妻回家，将王宝山非法关押到路南区拘留所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，唐山市国保大队伙同丰润区国保大队将王宝山劫持到丰润区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在没有任何法律依据的情况下，遵化法院以从王宝山家中非法搜查出的打印机、法轮功书籍及真相资料等物品为由，枉法判王宝山五年半，勒索罚金二万元。目前在河北省监狱管理局冀东分局第二监狱继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王毕红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">南京市溧水区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被永阳镇派出所警察抓捕、抢劫，在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被南京市雨花区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E6%B1%9F%E8%8B%8F%E7%9C%81%E5%8D%97%E4%BA%AC%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%A1%BE%E8%B6%85%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441615.html"><b lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省江门市法轮功学员。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被当地<span lang="EN-US">610</span>及警察抓捕抄家，关押在江门看守所。看守所期间，王斌被强迫检查身体，警察用几十斤重的一字形八十公分铁锁把他的双脚分开八十公分，强迫他带着锁上楼梯，致使他双脚流血，身体遭受严重伤害。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月后，日前，家属收到律师发来的江门市蓬江区法院《刑事判决书》，法院竟以王斌用<span lang="EN-US">VIVO</span>牌和中兴牌手机注册微信号建群传播真实消息为由，将他重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年并罚款人民币三万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王炳章：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1947</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河北省石家庄市籍人，基督徒，美国永久居民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年曾在美国创办《中国之春》杂志，被捕前任中国民主正义党发言人、中国民主党海外联合总部顾问；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被不明身份的人在越南绑架后带到中国境内被警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日以“间谍和组织领导恐怖组织罪”被判无期徒刑。据其家人称，王炳章的身体现在随时有生命危险，狱方已在囚室安放了警报器，要求其一旦感到有任何不适马上按响警报；其深知自己健康状况频危，已经写好遗嘱，希望“请加拿大牧师前往中国为他送葬，并要求做遗体解剖公布死因”。目前在广东省韶关北江监狱（广东省韶关市浈江区梨市镇<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号信箱<span lang="EN-US">6-9</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">512140</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王长青：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省庄河市法轮功学员。男，家住辽宁省大连市庄河市光明山镇魏屯，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在家中被抓捕，第二天回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日再次在家中被警察抓捕，之后遭当地中共公检法人员的司法构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份被大连普兰店法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，现在被关在普兰店看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/12/449486.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王春艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市南岗区征仪花园小区法轮功学员<b>。</b><span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被抓捕、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，以“取保候审”名义回家，后又被抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，哈尔滨铁路法院对王春艳判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，王春艳现被关押在哈尔滨市看守所（鸭子圈）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/8/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436585.html#2217234049-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王翠英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东菏泽市牡丹区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，原中共菏泽市委党校干部，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年退休。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年度，被评为“全省系统先进工作者”，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年度评为“全市系统先进工作者”，并全票通过副处级干部提拔。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日傍晚，王翠英在路边发送法轮功册子时，被跟踪监控的牡丹区公安局警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，王翠英被带入法庭，庭审期间，手铐、脚镣一直没有给卸掉。王翠英现在仍被非法关押在菏泽市看守所<span lang="EN-US">.2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉王翠英已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款两万元。家人去找审判长范虹要判决书不给，判决书内容、文号一律不给说，整个过程支支吾吾、闪烁其词，反复询问才得知其实三月十八日已经下达判决书，并说王翠英已提出上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王登朝：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，陕西省武功县人，前深圳市公安局罗湖分局三级督警，曾任深圳市保安公司第七公司经理，民主活动人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，因在深圳市莲花山公园准备组织一个为纪念孙中山逝世<span lang="EN-US">87</span>周年而做的民主宣传活动，而于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被拘押；随后又指控他在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年负责深圳大运会保安工作时，涉嫌虚报保安人数贪污<span lang="EN-US">283</span>万元，被深圳警方正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底，被深圳市罗湖区法院以“贪污罪”和“妨害公务罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年经二审改判，“妨害公务罪”被取消，贪污数额被减为<span lang="EN-US">80</span>万元，刑期减至为<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年有期徒刑。目前在广东省深圳巿监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王东吉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王敦龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">安徽合肥市法轮功学员被冤判入狱。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，王敦龙和妻子胡学业、妻姐胡文业，被合肥市瑶海区龙岗派出所和瑶海国保大队人员入室抓捕，并被抄去电脑、打印机、法轮功资料。随后，胡学业被拘留<span lang="EN-US">13</span>天，胡文业被“取保候审”。王敦龙被刑事拘留，后被批捕，一直被关押在合肥市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日其被合肥市蜀山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月、并罚金<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元，上诉后被维持冤判，他于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被转入到安徽省宿州监狱服刑。王敦龙家属收到宿州监狱通知，据说目前只要是修炼的家属一律不给会见（远程）、不准写信、不准打电话。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/27/2022-6-27.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/27/2022-6-27.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王凤花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省任丘市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在集市上告诉人们如何在瘟疫中自救保平安，被任丘市青塔乡派出所关押两天，家属被勒索钱财二十多万元，于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日回家，但仍然被构陷，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日从家中被绑架到了任丘市看守所，后被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王凤芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王甘霖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省阆中市人，江苏省南京市常住居民，原多家媒体记者及相关负责人；原“磅礴新闻”总编辑，著名调查记者，资深媒体人，坊间誉为“中国实力派调查记者”，异见媒体人，中国在押政治犯。早年大学阶段，曾通过自学考试攻读大学本科法律专业；毕业后进入新闻媒体行业，并逐渐成为多家媒体知名调查记者和媒体负责人；曾因在业界以擅长调查性报导和涉法报导着称，而被安徽卫视《记者档案》栏目在<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日以“调查记者王甘霖”为题进行专题报导，并从此人称“中国实力派调查记者”；但因其秉性率真耿直，故在媒体圈内颇有争议，并曾与另一媒体人因理念不合而公开对撕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因将国内<span lang="EN-US">6</span>家媒体和网站（后又追加百度、新浪网）先后告上南京市江宁区法院和南京市中级法院，故而引发社会广议；又因其刊发过不少轰动性调查报导，并且因此而推动过不少案件进展，遂得罪许多相关人士；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-17</span>日，其突然失踪，后得知因一篇监督报导而引发牢狱之灾，被江苏省邳州市警方莫名跨境抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日（或更长时日），被连续两次指定居所监视居住（实为秘押）；秘押期间，曾惨遭酷刑虐待；曾被坐老虎凳<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天，即第一次监视居住期间，被连续坐老虎凳<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天，第二次监视居住期间，被连续坐老虎凳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天；曾被持续<span lang="EN-US">36</span>个小时不让吃任何食物，以致因患有严重糖尿病而使其身体变得极度虚弱；后又被江邳州市警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转为拘捕，指控其因与另一位张姓媒体人“自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年以来，使用‘獬法’和‘等辩’等系列自媒体账号，以营利为目的，对鲁、晋、贵、粤等省的重大刑事案件及党委政府进行负面炒作，从事有偿发贴、散步虚假信息和有偿删帖等”，所以其言行已构成“非法经营罪”，应予以逮捕判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案在江苏省邳州市法院开庭审理，次日，因辩护人向法院提出了管辖权异议及请求排除非法证据、调取监视居住期间录像的申请，遂法庭只好宣布休庭。目前被羁押于江苏省邳州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_66.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_66.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王刚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1958</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，河北省人，原河北工程大学临床医学院副教授，人类党网站（或人类党论坛）作者<span lang="EN-US">, </span>笔名“诺亚方舟”，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。十几年前，曾因发表多篇评论时政及反思文革的文章，而被其任职大学所在地河北省邯郸市当局视为重点监控对像；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，又因质疑中共享人制度及专制腐败现像等，发表《致中共中央的公开信》，呼吁政治改革，而被邯郸市丛台区警方贴身监控；后因其不惧危险，仍旧经常在微信上发表批评政府的文章，而曾被邯郸市警方处治安拘留<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次（第一次拘留<span lang="EN-US">19</span>天，第二次拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天），被喝茶<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多次；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因再次呼吁中共反腐和政改等，后又于同年创立“上海百姓维权”与“中国百姓维权”等微信群，表明中共绝不会走民主宪政之路，故而呼吁“民众移民”，但此言行被警方获悉，遂立遭丛台区联西派出所警方的野蛮执法，并派专人以“科研助手”名义对其进行贴身监视；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，“六四”来临前夕，其频遭当地警方约谈和做笔录，并被威胁称，若其尽快退出微信群，且不再在网上发表违规言论，就不对其翻旧账，但若继续发声，不仅会被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10-15</span>天，更会将其以前的案子推翻，再以“颠覆国家政权罪”论处；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其突遭警方立案侦查，并由公安部统一部署，在全国五六个省份（如闽、粤、湘和海南等省） 对其展开调查；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被邯郸市丛台区丛西派出所警方以约谈之名诱骗至派出所后失联，至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉，其已被邯郸市丛台区警方正式刑事拘留。目前被羁押于邯郸市第一看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉：因言获罪六四前遭中共当局以刑事拘留的原河北工程大学临床医学院副教授王刚涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日由邯郸市公安局移送检察院审查起诉。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/2022819.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/2022819.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_28.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_28.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王广学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，王广学等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，王广学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王国廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，天津市人，原天津市北辰区下辛庄村民，维权者王复春之父，“夏俊峰”式的维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其所在村庄举行村干部换届选举，有“恶霸村长”之称的黄双来欲求连任，但却遭村民反对；鉴于黄在任期间存在帐目不清、多占土地等严重问题，村民决定推举其子王复春和另一村民衡庆杰竞选村官，随遭到黄双来等人的忌恨、威胁恐吓和打击报复。由于黄双来一直认为其子王复春的参选是受其指使，并唯恐王国廷为人正直，在村中有极高威望，会影响他的村长连任，随心生恶念，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日带领几名打手（据称皆系黄的亲戚）闯进其家中肆意打闹，其子王复春闻讯前来劝阻并报警，警方却不出警；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，黄再次指派打手前去暴打王复春，并用枪托将其嘴巴打伤，无奈之下王等人二次报警，警方依然既不出警也不立案；<span lang="EN-US"> 5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，黄第三次带领<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人夜闯其家，对其实施肆意殴打，其子女家人及众多村民纷纷赶往现场，双方发生冲突；尽管王等人立即报警，警方依然消极不作为，结果在正当防卫过程中，致使黄和另两名打手被钝器击伤、死亡；尽管之后其主动自首，但其及其亲友等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人均被警方抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，经天津市中级法院秘密审判，其被以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，剥夺政治权利终身；鉴于判决明显与事实不符，其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，天津市高级法院被迫对其进行两次秘审，仍做出宣判：“维持原判死刑，立即执行”；其不服继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月王复春与衡庆杰二人死刑复核通过并执行。王国廷重新庭审量刑。后王国廷被改判死缓。目前被羁押于天津市北辰看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省昭通市人，基督徒，云南省昭通市永善苗族教会神职人员，昭通市昭阳区城区基督教堂牧师，中国在押良心犯。自中共执政以来，一直对基督教等及其信徒进行严厉打击逼迫， 王海虽为官方教会认可的神职人员，曾于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2012</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日在昭通市昭阳区城区基督教堂按立牧职，但依然被云南当局视为需要秘密监控的对象；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，因其恪守基督教正宗教义信仰，拒绝与官方妥协合作，为迫其就范，其父母竟遭恐吓要挟；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，其被昭通市昭阳区警方莫名带走，自此失联，其父母亦被秘密关押；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，因其渺无音讯，其妻被迫在微信朋友圈发出求救信息，呼吁外界社会给予关注祈祷；截至目前，其及父母均长期下落不明；据悉，因家中老小均要抚养照顾，其妻正面临极大经济压力，且恐其被人暗杀。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王海干：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川达州市大竹县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，四川省达州市大竹县竹阳镇骨干教师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始迫害法轮功后，王海干多次被抓捕、关押，长期遭受中共邪党的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月起，因进京和平请愿、说明法轮功真相，被劳教两年。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾被劫入大竹看守所关押，次日被五花大绑，挂牌子，全城游街示众。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，被国保大队警方劫入四川省资阳大堰劳教所劳教两年。屡遭非人道虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，再次与多人被大竹县公安局、达州市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”等抓捕，关押在大竹县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被大竹县法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。上诉到中级法院，被维持原判。现在四川省嘉州监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/12/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%95%99%E5%B8%88%E7%8E%8B%E6%B5%B7%E4%B9%BE%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%98%89%E5%B7%9E%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-430719.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/12/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%95%99%E5%B8%88%E7%8E%8B%E6%B5%B7%E4%B9%BE%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%98%89%E5%B7%9E%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-430719.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王海芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，王海芹等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，王海芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 297.0pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王颢达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">25</span>岁吉林辽源公民。香港人民的反送中运动实际上得到许多大陆人民的支持，中共当局恐香港事态影响内地，一方面严密封锁消息，删帖删号封群，严密封杀消音；另一方面，对公开表达支持的网民则迅速抓捕，有的被刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">25</span>岁吉林辽源公民王颢达在微博上发布蒙面、独眼，倒拿五星红旗，手持打火机的照片，随后即刻遭辽源警方抓捕刑拘。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安市鄠邑区法轮功女学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生。法轮功女学员王红、董玉英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在鄠邑区将村镇附近讲真相时，被人恶意举报，被将村镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。王红因检查身体不适，被放回家。两人都被构陷到检察院、法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月西安市莲湖区法院非法庭审两名法轮功学员，王红坚持自己无罪，为自己做了有理有据的无罪辩护。王红保外就医在家，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日王红被蒋村镇派出所与鄠邑区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>警察在家绑架，现在被非法关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。后王红被西安市莲湖区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王洪霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省嫩江县九三农垦局荣军农场法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生。王洪霞、于桂荣<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日发放真相资料，被警察跟踪，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在于桂荣家被嫩江县公安局不法警察绑架，被关押到齐齐哈尔第二女子看守所。（这是王洪霞、于桂荣两人第二次同时遭绑架、构陷，被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，她们两人被绑架，于桂荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，王洪霞当时也被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，黑龙江省嫩江县法院判处王洪霞<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王红霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，四川省资阳市安岳县人，绰号小莲、小梅、小吴、莲姐，安岳县安岳镇铁峰路<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号居民，前安岳县教师进修学校英语教师，茶叶生意经营者，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信徒，中国在押良心犯。因信仰和长期锻炼、宣传法轮功屡遭四川当局的逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，曾因锻炼法轮功而被资阳市当局以“利用邪教组织扰乱社会秩序”罪由分别劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年（三次共计<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年半），劳教期间曾屡遭酷刑折磨；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因外省法轮功友人到成都做茶叶经销考察，当与其会面时被突然出现的成都市便衣警察以“是吸毒犯”为借口强行带走，并先后送到新津洗脑班、二娥湖洗脑班关押；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被资阳市安岳县警方以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”予以逮捕，并关押于资阳市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被四川省资阳市简阳县法院以同罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年；其不服提出上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经四川省资阳市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月；据悉，曾在狱中因绝食抗议而致身体枯瘦如柴，生命垂危；其家属探监权（含约见律师）等遭禁。目前在四川省成都女子监狱六监区服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">王红香</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺东洲法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁高龄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午王红香在东洲区搭连集市，被龙凤派出所抓捕，后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月家属得知王红香被东洲法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押在抚顺市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王宏滨：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。一九七一年出生。因坚持信仰真善忍，遭到中共多次绑架，被非法劳教、非法判刑，共计冤刑逾二十年。他曾于一九九九年被劳教，刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年，王宏滨遭抓捕后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，被关押在马三家监狱。出狱后仅四年，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，王宏滨再次遭绑架。当日他正在家睡觉，被闯入的双城公安局警察抓捕、抄家，之后又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。在监狱中这些年，王宏滨身体一直不好，近期血压高达<span lang="EN-US">280</span>～<span lang="EN-US">300</span>。有狱警捎信说：“王宏滨状况很不好，已经在安排自己的后事了。”家属找相关部门要求办理保外就医。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，监狱七监区赵姓队长给家属来电话声称，他们没有迫害王宏滨，让他去医院看病他不配合。而据出狱犯人提供的信息，在监狱，王宏滨被迫害得非常严重。在外界打电话和家属介入的情况下，六月六日，狱警带王宏滨去了公安医院，也没通知家属。七日，又转回呼兰监狱。王宏滨入狱三年多了，狱方一直不让家属探视和打电话，完全剥夺了监狱明文规定的在押人员及其家属的基本权利。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/12/444805.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/12/444805.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王厚积<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省大连法轮功学。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，在大连地区对法轮功学员的集中抓捕行动中，王厚积被八一路派出所警察抓捕。后悉，王厚积遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441619.html#22422221331-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441619.html#22422221331-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王吉梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆市渝北区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日王吉梅被捕，被关押在渝北区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月得知她被江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447801.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447801.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王建：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1950</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日王建被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王建兵</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年生，甘肃天水人，独立公益人。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年大学毕业后，便加入北京西部阳光农村发展基金从事农村发展工作，开启长期关注青少年教育及成长的公益职业生涯。曾担任西部阳光基金会农村教育项目主管<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年加入广州恭明社会组织发展中心，作为青少年成长项目和残障社群赋能项目主管及统筹，支持和发起相关社区项目工作。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年起开始关注职业病工人的权益倡导和服务性工作，提供必要的法律支持。王也是国内<span lang="EN-US">MeToo</span>运动中重要的支持者。王建兵原计划<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日送别女权记者黄雪琴经香港赴英国留学。但是，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">,</span>广州警方于王建兵出租屋中<span lang="EN-US">(</span>位于广州海珠区新港西路<span lang="EN-US">)</span>强行将王建兵和即将出国留学的黄雪琴一同抓走<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并查抄了两人的私人财物。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">,</span>王建兵的朋友于黄埔长洲用于储物的出租屋也遭到警方强行撬锁进入搜查<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并带走大量物品和行李箱。据知情人士透露，目前可以确认两人系被广州警方控制，警方均以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”拘留了王建兵和黄雪琴两人<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并疑对双方采取了“指定居所监视居住”措施。主要原因是涉及日常在王建兵他家中的朋友聚会。警方拒绝告知亲友二人具体下落。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王建兵家属收到广州市公安局发出的“逮捕通知书”，逮捕公函号为特殊的穗公捕通字<span lang="EN-US">[2021]X2</span>。该通知书显示王建兵已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被广州市公安局以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权”的名义被执行逮捕。黄雪琴、王建兵于<span lang="EN-US"> 2022 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 27 </span>日正式移送广州市检察院审查起诉。此前黄雪琴曾在未通知家属与律师的情况下，被私下转移至疑似广州第二看守所处单独关押审讯数月，而王建兵也曾被单独关押于其他场所审讯数月。目前二人已重新转至广州第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_1.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_1.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王建敏</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山东省烟台地区莱阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，山东烟台莱阳市柏林庄卫生院退休医生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，王建敏在莱阳市联通公司大门东侧邮箱投递法轮功信后，被莱阳公安跟踪绑架。傍晚，王建敏被抄家，警察抢走了大量私人物品，包括真相币、真相资料、电脑、打印机等，具体数目不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王建敏即被关押到烟台市看守所，刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王建敏被莱阳市公安局非法逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，烟台市中级法院一审判王建敏<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王金凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁沈阳法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。因坚持修炼法轮功，王金凤多次遭到中共迫害，被长期骚扰、拘留、洗脑班迫害，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被康平县法院判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在辽宁省女子监狱关押期间，王金凤遭到各种酷刑虐待和非人折磨。王金凤和李凤芝于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被皇姑区黄河派出所、皇姑区国保警察抓捕构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，沈阳市两位善良妇女王金凤、李凤芝坚持修炼法轮大法真、善、忍，被于洪区法院判刑：王金凤<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，李凤芝<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，各罚金五千元。王金凤刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/4/450397.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大庆油田公司采油五厂法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已八十岁。原大庆石油管理局申大公司职工家属，家住红岗区采油五厂。她于一九九八年修炼法轮功，身心受益。一九九九年七月二十日，中共疯狂打压法轮功，残酷迫害法轮功修炼者；王景翠曾多次被绑架、抄家、关押，经济勒索、一次被劳教，三次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被红岗区公安分局警察抓捕，被大庆市萨尔图区高新开发区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款一万元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年过完年，她被转入到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害，这已是她第三次被诬判入狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王景丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">哈尔滨市双城区人，法轮功学员。在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年对法轮功的迫害过程中，她曾在看守所、劳教所、洗脑班、派出所被关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区公安分局建国派出所抓捕抄家，被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所；当天哈尔滨南岗区、道里区、道外区、香坊区、松北区、双城区<span lang="EN-US">17</span>名法轮功学员被警察抓捕、抄家、骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因传播法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日下午，王静慧在一个封闭小区发放法轮大法好的资料，被沈阳市公安局于洪分局北陵派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，法轮功学员王静慧被沈阳市于洪区法院视频开庭。近日获悉，她被于洪区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省成都市东华机械厂退休职工、法轮功女学员。王敬琳<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在家中被派出所警察抓捕，两所住房被警察抄家，大法书籍、真相资料、电脑、现金（约<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元一元真相币，还有金额不清的美元）等被警察抢走。据悉王敬琳在成都机投镇某小区发真相资料被构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被开庭，当庭未宣，于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王聚才<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后王聚才被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，王聚才刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生，农民，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆（洗脑班），被铐在铁椅子上（除上卫生间外）一天二十四小时不让下来，来例假也不例外；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，宝鸡市金台区法院给下达起诉书及监视居住六个月通知。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王军平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北石家庄市鹿泉区石井乡栈道村维权人士。因王军平的工人被无缘无故居打成重伤，王军平自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>起到北京中南海周边上访<span lang="EN-US">13</span>次拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，王军平去镇政府上访，镇长让司机开车离开，王军平到镇长车前要求镇长答复，镇长的司机就殴打王军平。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，王军平在亲戚家被欺骗回家以寻衅磁事刑事拘留，后被起诉。此案<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日在法院开庭，未判决。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王君洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁康平县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，家住辽宁省沈阳市康平县东关乡。在天津市滨海新区生态城当保安。因修炼法轮功曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。王君洲在天津市滨海新区生态城当保安，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日（或<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日）下班时，被滨新区生态城分局警察抓捕，据说是因为在微信中转发香港反送中相关信息。在王君洲被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被天津市滨海新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王克民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王蕾</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：女 ，北京西城区法轮功学员。王蕾因发放法轮功材料，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午其家被西城派出所和国保抄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，王蕾北京西城区德胜门外派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日二次开庭。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，二审维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://library.minghui.org/victim/i127979.htm"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://library.minghui.org/victim/i127979.htm</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/9/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441084.html#2248211253-1"><b
