style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王丽东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁阜新市法轮功学员。王丽东、宋跃武夫妇在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日遭抓捕，近期获悉两人已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已经从看守所送走，送哪个监狱未知。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/6/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-427523.html#21627232735-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/6/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-427523.html#21627232735-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王立芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王复春的母亲。因竞选村长，原天津下辛庄村恶霸村长黄双来对村民王复春参与竞选恨之入骨，多次带领亲信打手到王复春父母家逼其退选，二老也曾多次报警警方不管。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日夜间<span lang="EN-US">11</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>点钟，黄双来带<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人夜闯王国廷家，暴力威胁王国廷，不准其子王复春参选村长，与闻讯赶来的王复春及众村民发生冲突，黄双来等三人被殴致死。该案<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日一审，天津一中院将“聚众斗殴罪”改为“故意杀人罪”判处王复春、王国廷、村民衡庆杰死刑，王立芳被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月王复春与衡庆杰死刑通过并执行。王立芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王立恒</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">:1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，山东省淄博市桓台县人，淄博市桓台县果里镇马王村<span lang="EN-US">187</span>号公民；香港占中运动支持者，“恶俗维基”及“支纳维基”二网站骨干成员，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，中国大陆及海外有网友开始频繁尝试搭建和运作被称为“恶俗圈”的网络平台，其中“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”和“红岸基金会”三大网站最为知名；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年期间，其因与多人积极合作组建“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”二网站，随深受网站友人好评；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因香港“占中”、要求“真普选”运动遭到中共当局授意下的港府严打，同时中国大陆《人民日报》又连续第<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天刊文批评占中运动，随于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日毅然赴香港金钟占领区，在天桥顶撑伞支持“占中”的学生及市民；但返回后不久，即被淄博市桓台县警方刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又被山东省桓台县检察院以涉嫌“非法获取公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“侵犯公民个人信息罪”和“非法获取国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因其又重回恶俗维基网站工作，而此时已有多家“恶俗圈”网站频发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的信息（含户籍和照片等个人信息），其所在“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”网站亦将此类信息挂于网上，遂立遭中共当局的打压迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，公安部迅速成立项目组，要求对全国该网站会员实施大抓捕；之后经严格审讯，发觉他们年龄尚小且行为基本无罪，故而各地警方将所抓之人纷纷予以释放，唯广东省茂名市警方想立功，声称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，遂移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把该警局所属的网站会员（含其在内）尽都抓捕，并上报公安部谎称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被广东省茂名市警方跨省抓捕，并被指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等转刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被茂名市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪、侵犯公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；据悉曾因资料不足，而被检察院几次退侦和被地方法院数次退回要求重新起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”被广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，王立恒被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年），“侵犯公民个人信息罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月），二罪并罚，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；其等均表不服，已经上诉；二审维持原判。目前王立恒被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王利芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，云南省昆明市人，又名王丽，职业不详，著名自由派先锋诗人及作家王藏（本名王玉文）之妻，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自从与自由派先锋诗人、作家王藏结婚以来，虽低调生活，但仍因其夫是异见诗人屡遭北京、昆明等地当局牵连与恐吓；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾因其夫王藏被云南省楚雄市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”拘捕，而遭当局指使的不明人士抢劫，且被以若拒绝与警方合作，家即被逼迁和断水断电，甚至“会弄死孩子”等做要挟，致其因恐惧伤及<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个幼子而得精神分裂症；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因云南当局强行要求王藏一家从北京迁回云南昆明原籍，其又被不明人士威胁、殴打，故而精神再度失常，导致其抑郁症发作，严重时曾出现精神恍惚、昏迷不醒，离家出走甚至跳湖自杀等现象；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其夫王藏被云南省楚雄市警方突然以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”带走刑拘，自此失联，因其夫多日毫无下落，其被迫无奈，遂在各路网站（尤其是<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>）携子为丈夫被抓捕呼吁，以求正义人士广泛关注与声援，后得知其夫已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被云南省楚雄州检察院以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因其在<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>上为丈夫呼吁受株连，亦被楚雄州检察院以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”批捕；据悉，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个幼子被长期囚禁家中，除准予姥姥临时照看外，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>幼子已多日未见父母；友人恐其因此而使抑郁症倾向加重。目前被羁押于楚雄州看守所（云南省楚雄市鹿城镇福塔小区上平山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">675000</span>）。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，王藏（王玉文）、王利芹夫妇涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案遭延期审限，本案最后审限从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日再延期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，王利芹夫妇涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案代理律师张磊公开喊话云南省楚雄州中级法院：“<span lang="EN-US">@</span>楚雄中院 云南省楚雄州中级法院应当立即对王利芹取保候审，不说是冤错案了，不说她的身体状况了，不说她的四个孩子了，就说检察院对她的量刑建议立即就要坐满了，你们法院还不判，又不放，那就是你们法院责任人杜梅法官的个人问题了，那就是私人恩怨了。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省淄博市张店区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年四十多岁。因传播法轮功曾遭<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年冤狱。后<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月他再次被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在山东省监狱十一监区遭受了残忍迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/10/446050.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王林安：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西九江公民。<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年出生，退休人员，网名<span lang="EN-US">:</span>陶洼的铁鱼。因二十大维稳，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初，王林安在家写文章被国保带走，并带走了电脑等物品，没有给家人出示法律文书。打办案警察电话告知，行政拘留最多关押<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，但<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日期满未归，再次致电国保，告知已经刑事拘留，现关押在九江市看守所，家属不能会见，其可能与同为九江公民的李玉荣同天被抓。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">据悉，王林安身体体状況不好，国保多次通知家属送药到公安局。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名‘我在红尘你在天上<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>’。女，安徽人士，徽乡网总监，因于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日<span lang="EN-US">15</span>时通过新浪微博发布消息称：安徽颖上夏桥镇拆迁逼死老人，发微博的同时附有一段十秒钟显示，视频中显示有多名身着“特警”字样服装的彪形大汉，队形整齐，臂戴红色袖套，蒙着黑色头套，到一处疑似办丧事的地方“执法”。该视频早前已被微博官方删除。后王琳琳于在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索未遂”罪抓捕关押，后王琳琳因揭发熊德超领导下的颍上拆迁逼死老人、美好乡村虚假惠民工程，而被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。此案正在申诉中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王楣泓<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，王楣泓被牡丹江市爱民区中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害，曾多次遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年获释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日又被哈尔滨市南岗区公安分局哈西派出所警察抓捕构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院庭审。后获悉，王楣泓被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初投入黑龙江女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在昆明官渡区牛街庄圣马网吧旁被公安抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>华检察院出庭指控：王美玲在网吧路旁散发法轮功真相材料，在包中有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；王美卿被判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；刘新安被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王明海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; minor-fareast;">安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，遂遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，突遭冲击，被芜湖市戈江区警方闯入教学点，将包括其在内的十名老师悉数带走，教学点亦遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其十人被视为同案犯，统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被取保候审外，王明海及万红霞等另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名老师均被芜湖市戈江区检察院以同罪由正式批捕；据悉，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王明慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省雅安市名山区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日晚王明慧被名山区国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。后被关押在雅安天全看守所。王明慧于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，索罚金一万元。近两年后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被关押到成都龙泉驿女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/9/449149.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/9/449149.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王明全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃省庆阳市环县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年出生，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功，身心受益。王明全<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被环县环城派出所警察从家中抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，王明全被环县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">王朋影：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林省舒兰市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年近七十岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，王朋影多次被绑架，曾三次被劳教，一次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，王朋影出门办事，被警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所迫害。后获悉，王朋影被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王鹏义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁王。王鹏义是军队转业干部，在军队为国家服务多年，转业到抚顺市粮食局所属企业。在中共江泽民集团发动的对法轮功的迫害<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年中，王鹏义遭受了多次抓捕、劳教、判刑，受到多种酷刑折磨，九死一生，身心受到极大的伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，王鹏义失踪，经常与他在一起的亲友也联系不上他。一年半以后获悉，他又被抚顺市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现在在沈阳沈北新区康家山监狱二监区。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王平创：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市武功县法轮功学员。王平创<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日生，妻子赵西娟<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日生，陕西咸阳市武功县普集镇义老村人，近年在西安做生意维持生活。王平创曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被劳教迫害，在枣子河劳教所受尽酷刑，被关笼子、夏天暴晒、冬天被浇凉水、做奴工、被牢头暴打等，他一度被迫害致生命垂危。由于警察多次上门骚扰，王平创夫妻被迫流离失所在外。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，王平创夫妻骑电动车在本市公交站牌上粘贴 “法轮大法好”，遭人举报。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日夫妻俩遭周至县公安局和长安区郭杜镇派出所抓捕，参与的警察有<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多人，并抄家。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span>王平创、赵西娟夫妇在西安遭抓捕关押构陷近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">, </span>于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被雁塔区法院法官分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，共勒索<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万惩金。两人不服判决，已上诉至西安市中级法院。目前王平创被关押在西安市安康医院，赵西娟被关押在西安市看守所，两处均以疫情为由不让会见。王平创刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-%E7%8E%8B%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%9B%E3%80%81%E8%B5%B5%E8%A5%BF%E5%A8%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-441327.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-%E7%8E%8B%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%9B%E3%80%81%E8%B5%B5%E8%A5%BF%E5%A8%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-441327.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王齐花：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年六十六岁，家住武汉市新洲区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日上午十点多钟，村部会计何胜伢带领新洲区国保大队四人和旧街派出所一人，闯入王齐花家中，非法抄家，其中一人带着摄像机在家里到处摄像，来人看到王齐花家里挂的匾额十字绣艺术品（绣有法轮大法好和莲花），就强行摘下带走，还搜出几部旧手机，这群人就走了。后被新洲区国保大队和当地警察绑架到蔡甸区玉笋山洗脑班，几天后关到第一女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，武汉新洲区法院判王齐花八年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市东昌府区名法轮功学员。张淑萍、王芹<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被聊城市东昌府区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>、国保大队、柳园派出所警察等抄家。王芹被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月左右被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王清：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>河南省南阳市人，政府信息公开申请人，知名民间维权举报打假人，中国在押维权人士。十多年前，曾因向河南省南阳市“<span lang="EN-US">181</span>个政府部门申请信息公开”，引起社会热议，但被官方视为“河南刁民”；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，又曾因举报打假而被网络评选为“<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年十大公民”之一，自此其维权行为更是全国闻名；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因将有官方支持背景，且有违法经营操作的南阳市逸美时光咖啡店投诉到当地工商管理部门，期间虽经两次调解未果，但在其不懈努力下，最终迫使工商机关依法对该店做出罚款<span lang="EN-US">45000</span>元措施，并于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年向当地法院提出予以强制执行申请；然而其正义维权行为却因触碰了当地权贵集团的利益，遂遭官商勾结势力的打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，后被卧龙区检察院快速批捕，并被指控，因其在向各级工商管理部门进行投诉举报时有“威胁恐吓敲诈勒索商家”之嫌，故而触犯了政府相关法律；另有陈强、王聚才及韩猛等三名维权打假者亦作为同案犯被相继逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，另三人亦被分别枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年不等，并处罚金若干；其不服判决，立即提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，经南阳市中级法院二审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，目前被羁押于南阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王庆<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王庆英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，河南省济源市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，任召军的母亲。河南省济源市轵城镇西留养村人。河南省济源市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年生，河南省济源市轵城镇西留养村人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，济源市公安局“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”警察李建锋带领多人使用梯子翻墙跳入任召军家的院内后，又破门闯入任召军的房内，翻箱倒柜，抄走了电脑、打印机、手机、银行卡、银行存折、大法书籍以及其它部份财物等<span lang="EN-US">34</span>件，又绑抓捕了任召军及父母一家三人到济源市看守所。一个月后，父亲任宗禄被“取保候审”回家。任召军和王庆英被济源市检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年十<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，济源市法院宣布判任召军<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年刑期并且罚款二万五千元，判王庆英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月刑期并且罚款六千元。随后，任召军和母亲王庆英均上诉到济源市中级法院，但均被驳回，维持非法原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王庆英被遣送到河南省女子监狱，任召军仍然被非法关押在河南省济源市看守所。王庆英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王秋萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生。因修炼法轮功，王秋萍曾经被关押在马三家劳教所迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日因发放疫情周刊被一位武警恶告。送到马路湾派出所，搜走了随身带的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>千多元钱和手表、自行车和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>张封城期间的某小区通行证。由两个和平区国保大队的人连打带骂的审问，王秋萍不配合迫害，没报名，没签字，半夜逃走。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，再次被抓捕，送往和平区精神病院迫害。王秋萍被关押在精神病院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个半月多后，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被和平区国保大队、马路湾派出所警察送往沈阳市第二看守所迫害。看守所拒绝家人送衣物、存钱，更不许律师接见。王秋萍<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被关押到辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/10/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436647.html#2219223842-5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王荣军：</span></b><span line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年七十二岁；女儿那艳四十多岁，是沈阳市第六医院的护士。王荣军、那艳母女俩于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日左右失踪。亲朋好友到处寻找，从那艳工作单位，到派出所，到街道，没有任何人提供讯息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，亲属才得到母女俩被绑架并被判刑的确切消息。现在她们仍被非法关押在沈阳市第一看守所。王荣军及女儿那艳（那燕）已分别被辽中区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/22/443930.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王瑞玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日王瑞玲被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王瑞萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">：女，辽宁大连市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，被大连警方抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月下旬，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王尚杰：男，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波<span lang="EN-US">,4</span>人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判王尚杰<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王胜利：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，内蒙古自治区人，原中共党员，前内蒙古自治区公安厅刑事侦查总队警察，内蒙古自治区公安厅经济犯罪侦查总队侵害知识产权市场秩序犯罪侦查支队原支队长，蒙冤维权警察，反腐举报人。早年曾就读于内蒙古医科大学，但毕业后并未从事医生职业，而是选择继承父业，通过公务员考试进入公安系统成为一名刑侦警察；工作中，因曾侦办过许多大案要案，故而多次获得一等功、二等功、三等功等殊荣，并被评为内蒙古自治区优秀侦查员；然而，因其工作岗位的特殊性及其工作态度的敬业、认真性，让其看到经济案件侦查工作的复杂性与在巨额利益驱使下的人性脆弱、丑陋的一面；自<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年始，因拒绝与其上司王来明（内蒙古自治区公安厅原党委副书记、副厅长，以下简称“王”，已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日因涉嫌严重违纪违法而落马）媾和，利用职权助其贪污腐败、图谋私利，随成为王以案谋私的“挡路石”和仇视对象；后其虽对王之要求尽量选择疏远和回避，但终致被制造冤案，遭遇戕害；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被准格尔旗监察委员会以“因曾侦办过‘<span lang="EN-US">9.18</span>项目’（即王玉宝、常青等人合同诈骗案），有被‘保护伞’用以为此案犯罪嫌疑人‘做翻案工具’之嫌”为由带走，采取留置措施；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案被准格尔旗监委会以涉嫌“贪污、受贿和挪用公款”三罪向准格尔旗检察院提起审查起诉，之后曾被准格尔旗检察院以同罪由转正式批捕，但又因案件证据不足，曾有两次将其案退回侦补，三次延长审理起诉期限；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案再次被移送检察院审查起诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被自治区公安厅党委开除党籍、开除公职；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其案被准格尔旗检察院以涉嫌“贪污、挪用公款、受贿、巨额财产来源不明、滥用职权”等五罪向准格尔旗法院提起公诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被内蒙古自治区准格尔旗法院一审以“受贿罪；挪用公款罪、巨额财产来源不明罪、贪污罪；滥用职权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，立即提起上诉，坚称其所谓“罪行”并非真实，皆是“办案人员严刑逼供、编造罗织的产物”；后经鄂尔多斯市中级法院二审裁决，宣布撤销原一审判决，将案件发回重审；同时，因其身体极差，生命随时面临危险，随迫不得已准于取保候审出狱；但其为讨回公道，昭雪冤屈，一边取保在外治病，一边在网上发控诉信和遗书，公开举报王来明，称他才是纪检内鬼和真正的犯罪分子，并在幕后指使，致其终身残疾；同时，还通过各种合法途径持续向相关部门提交近<span lang="EN-US">80000</span>份《控告信》、《举报信》，虽都石沉大海，了无果效，但依然对外表明其已做好准备，誓将《遗书》、《控告信》和《举报信》留给家人、组织及社会，故而很快即被准格尔旗看守所收监；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案经鄂尔多斯中级法院三审，仍以受贿罪（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年），巨额财产来源不明罪（<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月），贪污罪<span lang="EN-US"> (1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">),</span>最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日；据悉，其母张仙花和两名亲戚因为其喊冤，竟也都被准格尔旗当局以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”拘捕；其中，其母于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被枉判刑期<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、缓期执行<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前被羁押于内蒙古自治区准格尔旗看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王淑波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江伊春市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，黑龙江省伊春市嘉荫县嘉荫农场退休职工，户籍所在地黑龙江省嘉荫县嘉荫农垦社区<span lang="EN-US">B</span>区<span lang="EN-US">9</span>委<span lang="EN-US">1</span>组<span lang="EN-US">246</span>号，现住址黑龙江省佳木斯市向阳区滨江小区<span lang="EN-US">2</span>期<span lang="EN-US">22</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">402</span>室。王淑波女士于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功，王淑波于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日傍晚，在佳木斯市住处遭向阳公安分局松林派出所警察入室抓捕、关押构陷，两次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，佳木斯市向阳区法院对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其被关押在佳木斯市看守所。王淑波上诉到佳木斯市中级法院，中院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被关押至黑龙江女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%8E%9F%E4%BC%8A%E6%98%A5%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E6%B7%91%E6%B3%A2%E5%9C%A8%E4%BD%B3%E6%9C%A8%E6%96%AF%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434327.html"><b 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%8E%9F%E4%BC%8A%E6%98%A5%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E6%B7%91%E6%B3%A2%E5%9C%A8%E4%BD%B3%E6%9C%A8%E6%96%AF%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434327.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王淑华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林松原市法轮功学员。为营救丈夫——松原市法轮功学员李国军，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日王淑华到长春市民康路派出所去要人，被非法扣押。后来得知王淑华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日送到兰家女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王淑敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，王淑敏被天津宁河公安分局、宁河芦台镇派出所、街道，联合抓捕，一直被非法关押在宁河区看守所，期间两次抄家。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王淑云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日在街上宣传法轮功，被站前派出所警察抓捕，被关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月她家属得知，王淑云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金两万元。法院开庭没有通知她家属。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E5%96%84%E4%BC%A0%E9%81%BF%E7%96%AB%E8%89%AF%E6%96%B9-%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E7%8E%8B%E6%B7%91%E4%BA%91%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-441353.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E5%96%84%E4%BC%A0%E9%81%BF%E7%96%AB%E8%89%AF%E6%96%B9-%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E7%8E%8B%E6%B7%91%E4%BA%91%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-441353.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王素平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王铁壮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，原南阳市工商局局长，法轮功学员。一九九九年七月法轮功被迫害后，当时法轮功学员王铁壮想为法轮功说句公道话，于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年进京上访，被当地公安接回后，南阳市市委书记、公安局长亲自作“转化”。他坚持法轮功，中共决定劳教他三年，把他关入河南省第三劳教所。南阳市政法委、公安局从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初对法轮功学员进行监听、监控，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份开始对全市所有住户、门店等进行名为入户走访，其实质是进入法轮功学员家中要户口簿、身份证、填表登记、照相。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日凌晨开始，在南阳市区以及各县开始大面积抓捕。王铁壮于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日也被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月王铁壮被南阳市宛城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款两万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王炜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">生于<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年。籍贯内蒙、中共党员。王玮于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被内蒙古赤峰市元宝山区警方刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被执行逮捕，关押在元宝山区看守所。王玮被抓捕前，系中共党员、国家公务员，在风水沟镇党建办公室工作。当局指控王玮自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月间，通过翻墙软件观看“大纪元”等法轮功节目，在推特上发表反宣特文<span lang="EN-US">40</span>余条，其中涉及支持、声援香港反送中运动，赞同法轮功观点，在境外网站发表“天佑香港——<span lang="EN-US">1</span>名大陆人对香港的祝福”、“退党声明”等文章。检察院在起诉书中以此建议对王玮从重处罚。后王玮被内蒙古赤峰市元宝山区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏国家法律实施罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，并被处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元人民币。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王威：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1990</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日出生，河南省周口市鹿邑县人，网名“自由大威”，广东省深圳市龙岗区阪田街杨美东四巷租住户，诗人、作家、独立媒体人，新公民运动团体“深圳公民联合会”创始人之一、龙岗分会会长，民主宪政追求者，人权活动人士，中国在押政治犯；近年来，因追求民主理念而对各种维权事件时有关注和探讨；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因与深圳公民邓洪成、肖兵、马志权、李南海等多人在深圳市五和餐厅聚餐谈论时政，席间肖兵和刚来深圳的江西公民李南海被深圳国保秘密拍照，次日中午，深圳市警方前往餐厅调查，拿着肖兵、李南海的照片要求工作人员指认，当天午后，其与邓洪成、肖兵、马志权、李海南等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人即被警方带走扣押，自此失联，另有深圳公民丁岩、王军、董凌鹏、王建华、宋立前、黄安阳等多人因参与共同聚餐，亦相继被失踪；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其被深圳市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”执行指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，又被深圳市检察院以同罪由正式批捕，且被关押在深圳市第二看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，被深圳市法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后送广东省英德监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因在微信群里公开发声援北京四通桥勇士彭立发倒习资讯，旋即被河南省周囗市鹿邑县警方留置扣押，至今未放。目前疑似被羁押在周口市鹿邑县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_45.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_45.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王卫真：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连法轮功学员、女、原沈阳军区大连高等医学专科学校内科教研室任教员，授衔上校，副师待遇。因坚持信仰、坚持讲法轮功真相，被中共当局多次骚扰、抓捕。每次抓捕都没有出示任何法律手续，比如搜查证等，完全是非法抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，在不通知任何亲属，法庭上只有陪送王卫真的儿子一人在场的情况下，中山区法院对她进行开庭审判。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，中山法院判王卫真<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年徒刑。后身体原因未入监。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，大连市中山区秀月派出所警察到家中抓捕了当时六十八岁的王卫真女士，将她强行劫持到大连市姚家看守所。人被送入看守所体检时，血压高至二百三十，但看守所仍然非法关押王卫真。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王卫真女士被押辽宁女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王文军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，绍兴市上虞区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮功。自一九九九年七月中共开始迫害法轮功后，王文军坚持信仰，长期遭受中共迫害，曾被判刑四年，被单位无理开除，十多年的工龄被清零，退休工资待遇被剥夺。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，绍兴市上虞区公安局国保大队和派出所警察闯到王文军家，破门而入，将她抓捕到派出所；第二天，家人被告知，她被“刑事拘留”；第三天家人又被告知，她被关押到洗脑班；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，王文军被嵊州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，罚金四千元。王文军被判刑后，即刻被关押到绍兴市上虞区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中旬获悉，王文军被关进浙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王西爱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东沂南县依汶镇隋家店村法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，沂南县公安局国保和依汶镇派出所集中骚扰和威胁王西爱的几个姐弟们，没有查找到王西爱的下落。后根据村里特务提供的信息，在依汶镇派出所所长刘伟明的带领下，十几名便衣警察，驱车到临沂市北城区，撬门开锁，将正在给儿子看孩子的王西爱抓捕，当日将她关押到临沂市河东区看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，遭沂南县法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王侠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省双鸭山市集贤县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，王侠（王霞）和牛玉杰两位女士在小区附近讲真相时，被不明真相世人举报，被福利派出所警察抓捕到派出所审讯、笔录。后王侠、牛玉杰二人被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被逮捕、关押在双鸭山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，集贤县法院对王侠、牛玉杰开庭，判王侠<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；牛玉杰<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月（经丈夫四处托人花了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>万元，并代写“三书”，现期满回家。）。王侠刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王霞<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省东营市东营法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，东营市公安局、分局、市国保支队、区国保大队及六户派出所、胜利派出所、新区派出所实施了抓捕，当时共有包括王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡在内的十多名法轮功学员被抓捕、抄家。其中，王霞因身体原因，被“取保候审”，崔桂芬、王沐怡两人被关押于东营市看守所。山东省东营市东营区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日对王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡进行开庭宣判。法官闫晓辉在没有任何法律依据的情况下对她们作出了非法判决。王霞被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款两万五千元；崔桂芬被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款两万元；王沐怡被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/3/2022-3-3.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/3/2022-3-3.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王香莉</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山东省临朐县法轮功学员。王香莉<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日在南京市江北新区儿子家，被南京市公安局江北新区分局盘城派出所警察抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，被江苏省南京市玄武法院冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款三万五千元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/1/15/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%94%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-418598.html#21114224852-3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/1/15/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%94%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-418598.html#21114224852-3</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王晓光：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾市籍人，原山西师范大学公职人员，基督徒，山西省临汾市浮山县金灯堂家庭教会主要负责人、牧师，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">"9.13"</span>山西临汾教案受害人，中国在押良心犯。王晓光笃信基督<span lang="EN-US">;</span>早期曾在山西师范大学任职，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年起，离职开始全职在教会做服侍工作，后成为金灯堂家庭教会牧师与主要负责人<span lang="EN-US">;</span>曾因着有《十架神学》等十几 部基督教神学著作，对中国家庭教会进行了深入分析，并根据马丁·路德的十架神学，提出了中国家庭教会十架神学四条原则，故而在 临汾家庭教会中备受尊重<span lang="EN-US">;</span>自<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年以来，在其夫妇（其妻子杨荣丽， 同为金灯堂教会传道人和主要负责人）与教会其他同工的共同努力带领下，其教会从几十人发展成拥有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名基督徒的大型教会<span lang="EN-US">;</span>正是基于其教会及影响力越来越大，随引起地方政府的强烈不满和恐慌<span lang="EN-US">;</span>又因其教会拒绝到临汾市民宗局登记，接受中共<span lang="EN-US">"</span>三自教会<span lang="EN-US">"</span>的管理，随屡遭打压，其养老金和医保待遇等具被取消<span lang="EN-US">;2004</span>年始，教会经常被临汾市当局断水停电<span lang="EN-US">;2009</span>年，曾因众信徒奉献<span lang="EN-US">1700</span>万元人民币建造了金灯堂大教堂，但其地址却被 地方当局看好搞开发，并称给<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>万元收购金灯堂，被其夫妇等教会负责人断然拒绝，故立遭报复性打压<span lang="EN-US">;2009 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">9 </span>月，<span lang="EN-US">"9.13"</span>山西临汾教案发生<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其夫妇等教会<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被临汾市警方刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，案件被检察院迅速移交至法院<span lang="EN-US">;2009 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被临汾市尧都区法院统一宣判，其中，其被以<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法占用农用地罪<span lang="EN-US">" </span>和「聚众扰乱交通秩序罪」判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；随后，其教会<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多个聚会点全部被封<span lang="EN-US">;2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因其与教会神职人员及众信徒一直拒绝将金灯堂转让给地方政府，随被浮山县政府以强行爆破方式夷为平地<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，将其等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>名教会神职人员和 同工悉数被抓捕，并被以金灯堂教会规模日益壮大，及家庭教会受洗不符国家规定等为由刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;</span>后部分人被取保释放，但其与其妻杨荣丽等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人仍被关押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被地方检察院以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>诈骗罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>予以批捕<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其案被移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">目前疑似被羁押于临汾市看守所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_92.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_92.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江牡丹江法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。原系黑龙江省烟草研究所高级农艺师，早在<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，因修炼法轮功，被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，关押在牡丹江监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，王新民被迫害出严重胰腺炎，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，被“保外就医”。在病情没有好转的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被牡丹江监狱以欺骗的手段，不顾身体情况，强行收监。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，才结束冤狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日又被抓捕，关押在牡丹江看守所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被爱民区法院开庭，王新民为自己做了无罪辩护。后王新民被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年王新民被牡丹江中级法院驳回上诉，维护原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，王新民被劫持到牡丹江监狱集训队继续关押迫害。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王秀红<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点钟，唐山丰润区公安局局长刘金良等有计划、有预谋抓捕丰润区法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、付瑞英、尉国申、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺、陆彩芸、韩玉芹、肖慧君等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁的法轮功学员韩玉芹当天被端明路派出所迫害致死。后来，耿福霞、付瑞英、尉国申以不同的病业形式返回家中；王秀红、陆彩芸、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺被转到唐山第一看守所遭受迫害。当时被抓捕的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员被构陷到遵化市法院。河北唐山市遵化法院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日对<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、尉国申、付瑞英、陆彩云开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日王秀红被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王雪祯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广州市越秀区法轮功学员，女，一九四四年九月出生，广东省药品监督管理局退休员工。一九九七年，她开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，广州地铁西塱站出现真相<span lang="EN-US">WIFI</span>信号，广州万联顾问有限公司练家伟到地铁黄沙站派出所进行恶告，黄沙站派出所于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日立案，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日广州市公安局公共交通分局对<span lang="EN-US">9</span>名法轮功学员实施绑架。王雪祯和儿子马民庆于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被抓捕，还抓捕其他七位法轮功学员，都被非法关押到广州市第一看守所。后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底转移到海珠区看守所，被迫害致无法站立，非法关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，王雪祯被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金五千元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已近七十八岁，王雪祯被诊断高血压、胸及腰椎体陈旧性压缩骨病以及腰椎退行性骨关节病，仍被关在冤狱中，正在接受治疗。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/18/445089.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/18/445089.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王学勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省东营市胜利油田法轮功学员，胜利油田孤岛集输大队职工，五十多岁，性情温和，为人很热心，工作勤勉，家中有一位贤惠的妻子和一个非常孝顺的儿子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日中午，王学勇被河口公安分局孤岛派出所国保大队四个警察，其中两个穿警服、两个穿便衣，非法闯入家中抄家、绑架。后他被刑事拘留、关押于河口看守所，后又转入牛庄看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在家属不知道的情况下，被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑。后被转入山东省监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王亚利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江鸡西市鸡冠区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，鸡西市鸡冠区十名法轮功学员遭黑龙江省公安、鸡西市警察绑架，二零二零年十月二十三日，王亚利被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王彦东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市绥中县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，绥中县国保大队副大队长刘唤宇等人，闯到高华家，抓捕了高华和高英姐妹，以及去串门的法轮功学员陈文艳和王彦东，抢劫了高华家的电脑、打印机等私人财物。高华被关押在葫芦岛看守所，高英被关押在葫芦岛拘留所，王彦东被关押在绥中看守所。陈文艳被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高华、高英、王彦东被构陷到绥中县检察院。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，高英回家，被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，高华、王彦东被构陷案到了葫芦岛连山检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日高华、王彦东被葫芦岛市连山法院判刑：高华<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，王彦东<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；王彦东刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434280.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434280.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王燕娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女。广东揭阳法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，她在揭阳市揭东区向民众讲述法轮功被迫害的真相时，被揭东区公安分局和城西派出所警察抓捕，关押到揭东区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年下半年，她被揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王怡：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，四川省三台县人，成都大学管理学院前讲师，“宪政论衡”网站创办人，作家，独立中文笔会会员，基督徒，成都秋雨圣约归正长老教会创办人、主任牧师， 中国在押良心犯。早年间，曾创立主持宪政网络论坛，研究中国宪政转型，因经常发表文章政论文章，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年被中国大陆当时以敢言着称的《南方人物周刊》评为“最有影响力的公共知识分子”之一；后成为基督徒，创立秋雨圣约教会，但因拒绝加入中共管控的“三自教会”，且教会信徒与日俱增，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其欲出境参加一个香港的宗教会议时，竟被中国海关以“出境有可能危害国家安全”为由禁止出境；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其夫妇二人又被成都市警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由带走传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，成都秋雨圣约教会突然被成都市警方大规模夜袭，百余名基督徒被以涉“寻衅滋事”、“非法经营”等罪名抓走，其亦被传唤；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被成都市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；之后尽管秋雨圣约教会立即发起全球信徒禁食祷告行动，抗议中共当局打压宗教自由，但至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日仍被成都市警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；据悉，其在被捕前曾发声明称，当局若将罪名指向其信仰、写作、言论和传教行为，他“将一概予以否认，服刑而不服法，伏法而不认罪”；其所在成都秋雨圣约教会于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日随即被成都宗教事务管理局发文予以取缔。目前被羁押于成都市看守所（成都市郫都区安靖镇正义路<span lang="EN-US">3</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">611731</span>）。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被四川省成都市中级法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“非法经营罪”，二罪并罚，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处没收个人财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王一飞：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，湖南省籍人士，化名小李，原网络秘密组织“兴中会”成员，网络秘密民运组织“兴华会”创建者和主要推动者，中国曾押政治犯。多年来一直低调并积极从事民主运动，因创建并与异议人士曾国凡等多人积极推动网络组织“兴华会”，倡导国内民众成立公民圈，开展启发民智的行动，而深受江西当局严控打压；因该会成员及支持者在南昌、赣州等地多处建筑物上喷涂“官员财产公开，人民代表直选”、“平反八九六四，结束一党专政”、“六四英灵，永远安息”等官方敏感标语，其宣传标语落款为“兴华会”，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其与曾国凡夫妇随被南昌市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”悉数带走、刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被南昌市警方以同罪由正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年某日，被江西省南昌市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，刑满释放。此前在江西南昌市洪都监狱服刑。王一飞<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日后微信朋友圈停止更新、微信公共号“一飞上天”则停在了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，最后一篇是“从看守所被解送到监狱服刑的纪念日”，至今失联一个多月，已遭抓捕。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/20_7.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/20_7.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体;
