style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴风桃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九六四年一月出生，家住揭阳普宁市流沙镇白沙陇村。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，吴风桃被普宁市公安局和大南山派出所警察抓捕，关押到普宁市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，法院到普宁市看守所宣判，吴凤桃被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吴淦：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，福建省福清市人，网名“屠夫”，退伍军人，知名维权围观者、人权捍卫者。近年来因频繁出现于诸多社会热点事件最前沿（如邓玉娇案、钱云会案、云南昆明小学生卖淫案、夏俊峰案等）而成为当局急于被维稳、打击的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年曾因为邓玉娇案和云南昆明小学生卖淫案网上维权， 而一跃成为网路知名维权围观者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月曾因福州市晋安区政府对王庄地区进行征地强拆，其拟以杀猪宝典行为艺术进行维权声援，而被当地警方抓走训诫。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因关注呼吁当局彻查披露庆安枪杀徐纯合真相，令当局十分恼火，而对其实施威胁，迫使其被迫逃离北京。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，又因声援江西乐平死刑冤案，并以“卖身筹款”的行为艺术举牌帮助律师在江西高院门前争取律师阅卷权，而被江西省南昌市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被福建警方以涉“寻衅滋事罪”、“诽谤罪”刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被厦门市检察院以涉“寻衅滋事罪”和“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日获悉，其案件已被转交天津警方处理。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日其案被天津巿第二中级法院秘密开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日终被该法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。羁押期间，曾累受酷刑折磨，甚至被强迫去住院进行“虐待式治疗”，为此，其不得不通过律师发出个人四不声明，以表明自己绝不自杀、不接受官方指定律师、不认罪和不上官媒悔罪的决心。目前被羁押于天津市第二看守所<span lang="EN-US">D101</span>室。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴刚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日出生，天津市和平区人，天津市某中学教师，抗强拆维权公民，中国在押维权人士。早期吴刚曾因其住宅被天津地方政府强拆，后其工作岗位又遭辞退，随被迫走上维权上访之路；近年来，曾因参与多起维权活动，尤其是参与声援天津北辰抗暴维权者王国廷案被当局枉法重判、维权公民在天津市人大门前举牌进行和平请愿等，而遭当局多次拘捕打压：<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日吴刚曾被天津警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月又被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日再次被警方以涉嫌“扰乱单位秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，吴刚再次因参与维权抗争而被天津市和平区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被以同罪名转正式逮捕，关押在天津市南开区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，吴刚案件在天津市和平区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被天津市中级法院第两次庭审，终以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，吴刚刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，因吴刚一直要求约见区人大代表，遂于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬突然失踪；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，知其被天津市河西区大营门派出所警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。目前被羁押于天津市河西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_75.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_75.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴京圣：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月出生，曾用名吴海古，浙江省衢州市人，早期职业原为教师，后成为自由职业者，六四亲历者，维权公民，民主人权斗士，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于浙江师范大学；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因给学生收听美国之音、台湾的亚洲之声播放六四真相，而被浙江当局知晓和很快拘捕，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被衢州市法院以“反革命宣传煽动罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日刑满出狱；后其为谋生计而移居北方，常年在河北省廊坊市三河市燕郊镇以开“摩的”载客为生，一直独身；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾因在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群里转发声援民主人士许志永的联署签名信及访民图片，而被北京市房山区警方以“编造传播虚假恐怖信息罪”刑拘，并关押于北京市房山区看守所，后被取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，曾因其坐在摩的驾驶座上怒斥城管的视频被人发于网上广传，而被河北省三河市警方以不确罪名抓捕，并被关押于河北省三河市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因在微信群、脸书（<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>）转发声援北京四通桥勇士彭立发贴文，而被当地派出所警方立刻喝茶；后虽被释放回家，但因其在脸书上又发被喝茶经过，称皆因把彭义士的标语图片编辑发到微信群里及个人界面而被监控，并表明将继续声援彭勇士及其贴文，以唤起更多人的心智，遂于次日（<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日）被老家浙江省衢州市衢江区警方抓捕，自此失联，涉嫌罪名暂不明晰。目前疑似被羁押于衢州市衢江区衢州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_28.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_28.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴玲娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会同工、基督徒。山西临汾金灯堂教案受害者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，山西临汾金灯堂教会九位负责人和同工被警方抓捕，其中包括曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的王晓光牧师和他的妻子、曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。据悉，批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴美芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东清远的失地农民维权代表。其所在的连州市丰阳镇其美村因为修高速公路需要征地，原村里负责人于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年趁村民外出做事，冒充村民在征地协议上签字，并侵吞集体土地征收补偿款。正在外面打工的其丈夫郭雪来接村民电话，立即回家和村民一起到镇政府讨说法，结果刚到镇政府大门口，十几村民就被抓捕了，其中郭雪来被以“扰乱国家工作机关秩序罪”判刑三年！后吴美芬为了替夫伸冤而被迫上访。郭雪来说：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份我爱人在北京信访时，给我们地方政府接访的人骗回来，说要保护我们的合法权益，解决我们的合理诉求，一个月后我收到逮捕通知书，说她“涉嫌扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”关押在铅山县看守所，就是这样得到党和政府的“保护”。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，郭雪来接到连州市法院电话，问要不要给他涉嫌“扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”的妻子吴美芬安排援助律师，郭雪来很清楚，所谓援助律师实际上就是官派律师，纯属为公检法“点炮”的，就断然拒绝了。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴启慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省绵阳市江油市法轮功学员。杜志俊、吴启慧夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被江油市公安局国保大队抄家，抢走电脑和所有大法书籍并被抓捕。杜志俊被抓捕到江油市看守所，吴启慧被抓捕到绵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，杜志俊被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半；吴启慧被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/17/445046.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/17/445046.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴婷婷</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山西临汾圣约家园教会财务同工。自<span lang="EN-US">8.19</span>山西临汾圣约家园教会教案爆发以来，临汾圣约教会两位传道人李洁和韩晓栋先是被指定居所监视居住，后被送往看守所，都以涉嫌“诈骗罪”而被批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日获悉：山西临汾圣约家园教会财务同工吴婷婷女士被控涉嫌“诈骗罪”而被刑事拘留。目前被羁押于山西省尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_30.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_30.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴文章：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。吴文章刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吴向洋：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年代后期出生，广西贵港市平南县人，网络工程师，网络<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>服务器搭建者，境外网站登陆软件服务商。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2010</span>年曾就读于中国人民大学，毕业后曾任职于腾讯科技（深圳）有限公司，辞职后自创企业“深圳千里通联科技公司”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2017</span>年，因在网上自己搭建<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>服务器并提供会员账号和登录软件，以供登录后可浏览境外网站，并将一些<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>会员账号密码写到硬件路由器上<span lang="EN-US">,</span>使得修改过的路由器能够直接登录<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>，以更好地实现可收听境外网站音<span lang="EN-US">/</span>视频节目的功能，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被中国当局网警获悉，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份被贵港市平南县警方刑拘。后被贵港市平南县检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”正式逮捕，控其在未取得《增值电信业务经营许可证》的情况下<span lang="EN-US">,</span>在网络上销售了<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>代理服务<span lang="EN-US">,</span>同时还利用“淘宝网”以开设网店和在互联网开设“凡狗<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>”网站等方式，向一般用户出租或销售<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>软件、<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>路由器硬件<span lang="EN-US">,</span>交易数千次<span lang="EN-US">,</span>非法经营额达<span lang="EN-US">792638</span>元<span lang="EN-US">,</span>非法获利约<span lang="EN-US">50</span>元，所以“根据《中华人民共和国电信条例》和《中国人民共和国刑法》等相关法律规定<span lang="EN-US">,</span>涉嫌非法经营罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月其被广西贵港市平南县法院一审以“非法经营罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前被羁押于广西平南县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴秀琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省白山市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，家住吉林省白山市靖宇县。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，吴秀琴多次被抓捕、关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱多次遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午，靖宇县公安局国保大队大队长于学军，闯入吴秀琴租住的公寓，实施抓捕、抄家、抢劫，并把她关押到白山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日吴秀琴被白山市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%99%BD%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E5%90%B4%E7%A7%80%E7%90%B4%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434439.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%99%BD%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E5%90%B4%E7%A7%80%E7%90%B4%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434439.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴旭钦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员吴旭钦<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日吴艳华与丈夫关兴涛被抓捕、构陷，后被大庆市让胡路区法院冤判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现在被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害。其丈夫关兴涛被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。吴艳华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴艳玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，王忠学、吴艳玲夫妇，均为凌源钢铁公司退休职工，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁。辽宁朝阳市凌源市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，朝阳市公安局，政法委，<span lang="EN-US">610</span>秘密开会策划迫害，预谋在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，要抓一批法轮功学员，向中共百年大庆“献礼”；并成立专项行动小组，电话监控，跟踪监视。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，朝阳市出动大批警力在同一时间对朝阳市法轮功学员及家属实施抓捕、抄家抢劫。据不完全统计，至少有<span lang="EN-US">27</span>名法轮功学员及家属被抓捕。凌源市公安局及派出所动用了大约<span lang="EN-US">50</span>名警察，抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名凌源市法轮功学员。王忠学、吴艳玲夫妇是其中两个，吴艳玲被关押在朝阳市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被凌源市法院远程视频开庭。后得知：吴艳玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/4/442063.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴永凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南洛阳工程造价师、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，她开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点多，洛阳市洛龙公安分局国保大队警察闯入吴永凤的家里实施抓捕、抄家，吴永凤和丈夫贺飞一同被抓捕到公安局，大量私人物品被抢走，家里留下两个十三、四岁的女儿。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被洛阳市洛龙区法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；她未修炼大法的丈夫贺飞被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年缓<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元；上诉到中级法院后，被驳回上诉维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/31/447052.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/31/447052.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴玉娟</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：女，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九七七年二月出生，揭阳市农科所法轮功学员。因张贴真相粘贴，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被榕城区公安分局警察抓捕，关押到揭阳市看守所。吴玉娟未修炼法轮功的丈夫也被拘禁了十天。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，她被揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金五万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴玉喜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北鄂州维权人士，湖北省鄂州市梁湖区太和镇花黄村上吴湾村民，因政府侵占其耕地和宅基地、剥夺其被救济权而上访，因上访吴玉喜长期被地方当局非法监控维稳。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，吴玉喜被地方官员从北京带回来后强制隔离了一次；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日辖区警察又上门要强行带她去隔离，在她坚持拒绝下没被带走。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日从北京带回后即被隔离关押的湖北鄂州维权人士吴玉喜的家属收到逮捕通知书。遂获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，吴玉喜被梁子湖区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕，现羁押在鄂州市公安局第一看守所。地址：鄂州市鄂城区葛山大道<span lang="EN-US">46</span>号。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_49.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_49.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吴泽衡：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，广东省揭阳市惠来县人，佛教徒，“华藏宗门”创始人，人称“行武禅师”，原“国际生命科学研究中心”香港总干事、亚洲部执行主席。自幼信仰佛教，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年起潜心学习并武术、兵法、医道等多元知识，后在少林寺拜高僧释德禅大和尚为师，研读经书，<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁已成为少林寺史上最年轻的总监坛；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年自创气功门派“华藏功”，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年更名为“华藏宗门”；<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年已在海内外颇具声望；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日曾撰文并上书《和谐社会的具体建议》，建议中共当局政治透明及对政治体制改革，因涉及信仰、党外监督、有限政府、选举等问题而被当局严控，后被刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被北京警方正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被北京市高级法院以“非法经营罪”、“擅自发行股票罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，并惨遭狱中酷刑虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获释后，其恪守信仰理念，再次发声坚称自己“对中华民族忠贞不渝，扶持正法，维护社会和谐统一”，且力推开展大型慈善活动，发起“辟谷行善、日行一善”，“公民互爱运动”等活动；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日曾因国际宗教自由委员会认定其为<span lang="EN-US">88</span>世佛教直系传人，并接到多个国际宗教组织的访问邀请，而被当局拒发出境旅游签证；随着中共当局近年来对宗教打压迫害程度的加强，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日其再次因政治及宗教信仰因素被珠海市警方以涉“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”刑拘，其住地被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日其被以涉“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”、强奸罪、诈骗罪和“生产、销售有毒、有害食品罪”四罪名提起公诉；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省珠海市中级法院以上述四罪名判处无期徒刑，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">715</span>万元，其宗教派别被定为邪教组织，二审后依然维持原判。目前其已从广东省四会监狱转送至新疆某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴志群：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1949</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，重庆市合川东津沱重棉四厂退休工人、法轮功学员。吴志群因发放法轮功<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，被不明真相的人恶意举报，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被国保绑架。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乌木别提•卡斯木（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁</b>，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><a name="_Hlk52050620"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邬成均：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，现年五十七岁，原本溪市钢铁公司工人，家住辽宁省本溪市明山区永新街。自中共一九九九年发动对法轮功的迫害后，他因坚持法轮功，多次遭中共抓捕、关押，他曾三次遭劳教，妻子也因他屡遭迫害而惊恐离世。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被当地警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被本溪市桓仁县法院判刑八年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日他被从辽阳市看守所转入盘锦监狱集训队（八监区）。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/21/445204.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/21/445204.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">伍健伟</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，英语名：<span lang="EN-US">Ng Kin-wai</span>，外号“<span lang="EN-US">K</span>先生”、<span lang="EN-US">Mr.K</span>，原英属香港籍人，现香港籍人，香港新界元朗区公民，前银行业职员，“天水联机”（属政治党派）主要组建人，前元朗区议会议员，中共眼中的“港独”分子，民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾在香港新界元朗区长大；大学毕业后，曾在银行业任职，并曾积极参与雨伞革命和“反送中”抗议活动（即反对《逃犯条例修订草案》运动）；后因元朗袭击事件，其认为亲中派议员垄断区议会，在重大议题上并未传递民间声音，故而联合多名于网上平台上认识的天水围居民组成政治党派“天水联机”，准备出战<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年香港立法会区议会选举；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，其以“天水联机”成员身份正式宣布并参选嘉湖北选区议会选举；期间，曾因和其他民主派元朗区候选人均有合作，故当民主党立法会议员、元朗区议员邝俊宇于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭歹徒伏击，遇袭受伤后，其立即与多名其他民主派人士共同联署谴责警方执法不公，要求港警公平执法；后经区议会选举激烈角逐，其最终击败原任亲中派议员李月民等参选人而胜出，并于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日正式任职；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因参与元朗袭击事件半周年集会之时，在元朗港铁站进行放映会叫市民毋忘事件之后，有大批防暴警察以查案为由前来围堵和抓捕与警方发生冲突的市民聚集者，其在现场劝架时，不幸遭警方胡椒喷雾喷中，并与天水联机”成员林进等共<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人一起被以涉嫌“组织未经批准集结罪”拘留；后其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人很快被释放，但再之后又被中共港府列为<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案之一，被香港国安处警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案被国安处警方指控涉嫌“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”，且大部分被告申请保释经香港高级法院<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天复核后，最终法官仅批准其中<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人以极严苛的条件予以保释，而其之申请保释被拒；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其与同党人林进在所属区的屯门裁判法院又被追加指控为“组织受禁群组聚集罪”，二人认罪被判罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天之后，其被辞任区议员职务；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其到香港高级法院再次申请保释，但被该院法官以“没有充足理由相信他不会继续实施危害国家安全行为”为由再次被拒，并指其仍需续押，以待再次被庭审聆讯；据悉，其因确信“颠覆国家政权罪”可被重判<span lang="EN-US">3-10</span>年，故在被法官拒保后曾呼吁：“香港人撑住，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年后再见！”目前被羁押于荔枝角收押所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_38.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_38.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52050620;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></span></p>
